##### Ikari Ikari no Mi (Anger)
*Devil Fruit, Uncommon*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.**  A blood red watermelon with black swirls, with vein-like protrusions across it.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to manipulate and harness the power of anger, making them an Anger Human. The user to fling themselves into a superhuman rage, or make others do so.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Mental Resistance.** You become immune to the charmed and frightened conditions.

**Reckless Anger.** By increasing your anger, you can throw aside all concern for defense to attack with fierce desperation. When you make your first attack on your turn, you can decide to a⁠ttack recklessly. Doing so gives you advantage on melee weapon a⁠ttack rolls during this turn, but atta⁠ck rolls against you have advantage until your next turn.

**Anger Amplification.** As an action, you can expend 1 devil fruit charge to amplify the anger within a creature within 60 feet of you. The creature must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature is affected by the Confusion spell for 1 minute, and deals an extra 1d6 damage of its weapon's damage type on each of its melee weapon attacks for the duration. At the end of each of its turns, an affected target can make a Wisdom saving throw. If it succeeds, this effect ends for that target, and it becomes immune to your Anger Amplifcaiton for the next 24 hours.

**Spells (Anger Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 5 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Wrathful Smite (1 charge), Compelled Duel (1 charge), Enthrall (2 charges), or Haste (3 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Rage Tempest).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to create a storm of anger in a 60-foot radius centered on you. Any creature of your choice within the area when it is first created must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or take 2d6 psychic damage and becomes consumed by anger, falling victim to the effects of your Anger Amplification for the duration. The creature can repeat this save at the end of each of its turns. If a creature succeeds on a save, it is immune to this effect for 24 hours. This awakening effect lasts for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. After using this ability, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.



```
```


##### Rubbu Rubbu no Mi (Friction)
*Devil Fruit, Uncommon*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** An orange kiwi type fruit with hair only on the pink swirls, causing the fruit to either feel rough or smooth depending on where you touch it.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to manipulate and control friction, making them a Friction Human. The user can increase or decrease friction within a certain radius.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Frictionless Fighter.** Thanks to your newfound abilities, you are completely immune to difficult terrain caused by natural environments, you have 10 feet of extra movement, and your movement speed cannot be reduced by your devil fruit's spells or abilities.

**Friction Control.** As an action, you can increase or decrease the friction within a 20-foot radius centered on a point you can see within 60 feet. The area becomes either high-friction or low-friction, respectively. If the area is high-friction, it becomes difficult terrain. If the area is low-friction, creatures move at twice their movement speed within the area. The effect lasts for 1 minute or until you use this feature again.

**Spells (Friction Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 5 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Decreased Friction (as Grease; 1 charge), Total Friction (as Hold Person; 2 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), or Friction Zone (as Plant Growth; affecting any area, not just plants; 3 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Friction Mastery).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to manipulate friction on a grand scale. You can increase or decrease the friction within a 120-foot radius centered on a point you can see within 300 feet, and the area becomes difficult terrain. A creature that moves inside the area or starts its turn in the area must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC if it moves into the area or starts inside the area during its turn. On a failure, if the area is frictionless, the creature falls prone, taking 2d8 bludgeoning damage, and cannot stand up for the rest of its turn, sliding in a random direction for up to half the target's movement, taking up it's full movement. Alternatively, on a failure, if the area has enhanced friction, the target takes 2d8 fire damage from the friction and is restrained until the end of its turn. Your allies are immune to the effects of this area. After using this ability, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.






CHAPTER 1 | UNCOMMON PARAMECIA

##### Garas Garas no Mi (Glass)
*Devil Fruit, Uncommon*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A shiny and clear cluster of crystal grapes, with silvery swirls on each grape. The stem itself is still completely visible.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to create glass out of any material, making them a Glass Human. The user can also transmute objects into glass objects, manipulate existing glass, and change the properties of glass.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Light Refraction.** You can control the air around you as if it were glass, allowing you to refract light in different ways. You learn the minor illusion and word of radiance cantrips, no material components required.

**Glass Transmutation.** As an action, you can make a Larger or smaller object, or up to a 10-foot area of an object or material, into clear glass. The object retains its durability and stats, but can be seen through by you and other creatures as if it is fully transparent glass. You can also make this glass one-way, only allowing creatures to see through it from one side, while the other sides are opaque when viewing it from a different angle, allowing for the user to spy on others very effectively. The effect lasts for 1 minute or until you use this feature again.

**Mirror Reflection.** As a bonus action, you can use 1 devil fruit charge to create a mirror-like surface on any glass object you can see within 30 feet, which lasts for 1 minute or until the object is destroyed. The mirror reflects light and can be used to blind creatures. Each creature which starts its turn within 15 feet of the mirror must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be blinded until the end of their turn.

**Spells (Glass Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 5 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Refractive Bolt (as Guiding Bolt; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Silent Image (1 charge), Mirror Image (2 charges), Refractive Beam (as Moonbeam; 2 charges), or Refractive Zone (as Spirit Guardians; radiant damage only; 3 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Glass Mastery).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to manipulate the refraction of light on a grand scale, allowing you to cast Sunburst, without expending a spell slot or material components . After using this ability, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.



```
```


##### Warau Warau no Mi (Laughter)
*Devil Fruit, Uncommon*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A rose colored lemon in the shape of lips, the swirls are a deep red like a nice shade of lipstick.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to manipulate laughter, making them a Laughter Human. The user can induce laughter in others, manipulate the volume and tone of laughter, and even use laughter to create shockwaves.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Mental Resillience.** You are resistant to psychic damage, as you are always in high spirits.

**Mocking Joke.** You learn the vicious mockery cantrip, forcing targets to laugh uncontrollably from your jokes. When a creature fails their saving throw against this cantrip when you use it, they also fall prone due to laughter.

**Laughter Manipulation.** You gain proficiency in the Performance and Persuasion skills. You can spend 1 devil fruit charge to gain advantage on any charisma check, as you induce a state of eurphoric laughter in creatures around you.

**Joyful Aura.** As an action, you can expend 1 devil fruit charge to create an aura of joy and laughter around you. For 1 minute, all creatures within a 10-foot radius of you have advantage on saving throws against being frightened and gain temporary hit points equal to twice your proficiency bonus at the start of each of their turns.

**Spells (Laughter Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 5 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Tasha's Hideous Laughter (1 charge), Calm Emotions (2 charges), Booming Laughter (as Shatter; 2 charges), or Beacon of Hope (3 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Laughter Overdrive).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to unleash an overwhelming wave of laughter energy. Each creature within a 30-foot radius of you must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature falls prone, becoming incapacitated with laughter for 1 minute, during which it can't speak or move. The creature can repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success. After using this ability, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 1 | UNCOMMON PARAMECIA

\page


##### Kiku Kiku no Mi (Hearing)
*Devil Fruit, Uncommon*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A white apple with peach coloured swirls going along it, the stem growing In a Volume symbol to represent sound.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to manipulate their hearing and the volume of sounds around them, making them a Hearing Human.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Hearing Aids.** You are immune to being deafened, and gain resistance to thunder damage.

**Enhanced Hearing.** You gain proficiency in the Perception skill, and you have advantage on Perception checks that rely on hearing.

**Tuning In.** You gain blindsight up to a range of 40 feet. As an action, you can amplify any sound you can hear within 120 feet. You can make a whisper audible to everyone in the area, cause a normal conversation to become deafening, or make a loud noise even louder. You can also focus your hearing to listen to a specific conversation or sound within range, even if it's behind a closed door or wall.

**Spells (Hearing Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 5 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Dissonant Whispers (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Silence (2 charges), or Shatter (2 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Sonic Resonance).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to create an intense sonic resonance in a 30-foot radius centered on you. Each creature in the area must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature takes 7d10 thunder damage, is deafened for 1 minute, and is knocked prone. On a successful save, the creature takes half as much damage and isn't deafened or knocked prone. After using this ability, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.



```
```


##### Snapu Snapu no Mi (Snapping)
*Devil Fruit, Uncommon*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A black pear-shaped fruit with a white crack down the middle. On both sides of the crack, the swirls seem to be going in opposite directions.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to create powerful elemental attacks by snapping their fingers, making them a Snapping Human. The user can unleash bursts of fire, bolts of electricity, or gusts of wind with a simple snap.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Deadly Snapping.** You learn the fire bolt, gust, and lightning lure cantrips, no material components required. 

**Elemental Snap.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to snap your fingers and choose one of the following elemental effects: Fire Snap, Electric Snap, or Wind Snap. Each elemental snap has a range of 60 feet and targets a creature or point you can see within range:

- **Fire Snap:** The target must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the target takes 2d6 fire damage and catches on fire. At the start of each of its turns, a creature on fire takes 1d6 fire damage. A creature can use its action to put out the flames, ending the effect.

- **Electric Snap:** The target must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the target takes 2d6 lightning damage and is paralyzed until the end of its next turn. On a successful save, the target takes half as much damage and isn't paralyzed.

- **Wind Snap:** The target must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the target takes 2d6 bludgeoning damage and is pushed 15 feet away from you. On a successful save, the target takes half as much damage and isn't pushed.

**Spells (Snap Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 5 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Chaos Bolt (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges),  Gust of Wind (2 charges), Fireball (3 charges), or Lightning Bolt (3 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Final Snap).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to unleash a massive elemental explosion in a 60-foot cone originating from you. Each creature in the cone must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature takes 5d6 fire damage, 5d6 lightning damage, and is pushed to the end of the cone and knocked prone. On a successful save, the creature takes half as much damage and isn't pushed or knocked prone. After using this ability, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.





CHAPTER 1 | UNCOMMON PARAMECIA

\page



##### Inu Inu no Mi, Model: Dalmation
*Devil Fruit, Uncommon*

**Type.** Standard Zoan

**Fruit appearance.** This devil fruit appears as a fuzzy white grapefruit with black spots covering its surface.

**Description.** This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a dalmation.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Beast Shape.** As an action, you are able to transform into a *Wolf* (reflavored as a dalmation) from the standard 5th Edition Monster Manual. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Hybrid Form.** You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Awakening.** Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.



```
```

**Fruit appearance.** This devil fruit appears as a lime green orange with darker scale-like patterns across its surface.

**Description.** This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a lizard.

##### Ushi Ushi no Mi, Model: Cow
*Devil Fruit, Uncommon*

**Type.** Standard Zoan

**Fruit appearance.** This devil fruit appears as a white watermelon with black blotches across its surface.

**Description.** This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a cow.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Beast Shape.** As an action, you are able to transform into a *Cow* from Volo's Guide to Monsters. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Hybrid Form.** You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Awakening.** Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

**Type.** Standard Zoan

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Hybrid Form.** You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Awakening.** Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. **Hybrid Form.** You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Awakening.** Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

___
> ## Giant Porcupine
>*Medium beast, unaligned*
> ___
> - **Armor Class** 12 (natural armor)
> - **Hit Points** 13 (2d8 + 4)
> - **Speed** 30 ft., burrow 10 ft.
>___
>|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
>|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
>|13 (+1)|10 (+0)|15 (+2)|2 (-4)|12 (+1)|5 (-3)|
>___
> - **Senses** darkvision 30 ft., passive Perception 11
> - **Challenge** 1/4 (50 XP)
> ___
> ***Keen Smell.***  The porcupine has advantage on Wisdom (Perception) checks that rely on smell.
>
> ***Quills.***  Any creature that makes a melee attack within 5 feet of the giant porcupine must make a DC 13 Dexterity saving throw or take 3 (1d6) piercing damage. Any creature that attempts to grapple the porcupine takes 3 (1d6) piercing damage when they make the attempt and at the start of each of their turns they maintain the grapple.
>
> ### Actions
> ***Multiattack.*** The porcupine makes two attacks: one with its bite and one with its claws.
>
> ***Bite.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +3 to hit, reach 5ft., one target. *Hit* (1d6 + 1) piercing damage
>
> ***Claws.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +3 to hit, reach 5ft., one target. *Hit* (2d4 + 1) slashing damage

___
> ## Giant Turtle
>*Medium beast, unaligned*
> ___
> - **Armor Class** 17 (natural armor), 12 while prone
> - **Hit Points** 13 (2d8 + 4)
> - **Speed** 25 ft., swim 30 ft.
>___
>|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
>|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
>|15 (+2)|10 (+0)|15 (+2)|2 (-4)|12 (+1)|5 (-3)|
>___
> - **Senses** darkvision 30 ft., passive Perception 11
> - **Challenge** 1/8 (25 XP)
> ___
>
> ***Stable.***  Whenever an effect knocks the turtle prone, it can make a DC 10 Constitution saving throw to avoid being knocked prone. A prone turtle is upside down. To stand up, it must succeed on a DC 10 Dexterity check on its turn and then use all its movement for that turn.
>
> ### Actions
>
> ***Bite.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +4 to hit, reach 5ft., one target. *Hit* (1d4 + 2) piercing damage

**Hybrid Form.** You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Awakening.** Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.



```
```

**Description.** This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a python.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Beast Shape.** As an action, you are able to transform into a *Constrictor Snake* (reflavored as a python) from the standard 5th Edition Monster Manual. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

# Rare Devil Fruits


##### Chiyu Chiyu no Mi (Healing)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A small pink cherry blossom-shaped fruit with intricate petal patterns.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to heal wounds and restore vitality through tears. The user can also accelerate natural healing processes in living creatures.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Healing Hands.** You have a pool of healing power that replenishes at the start of each dawn. With that pool, you can restore a total number of hit points equal to your level × 5. As an action, you can touch a creature and draw power from the pool to restore a number of hit points to that creature, up to the maximum amount remaining in your pool.


**Spells (Healing Tears).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Cure Wounds (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Lesser Restoration (2 charges), Aura of Vitality (3 charges), Greater Restoration (4 charges), Mass Cure Wounds (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Full Bloom).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Mass Heal without expending any charges or material components. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.



```
```






##### Choki Choki no Mi (Scissors)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A bright orange pineapple with an extra sharp rind and spiraling patterns across its surface.

**Description.** This fruit allows the user to transform any part of their body into scissors, which can be used to cut and manipulate objects and space as if they were paper. The user is also able to fold and transform objects or terrain that have been snipped.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Scissor Hands.** Your hands can transform into scissors, granting you the ability to cut through nonmagical materials effortlessly. Your unarmed strikes deal an additional 1d6 slashing damage. You deal double damage to structures and objects with your unarmed strikes.

**Material Cut.** As an action, you can make an unarmed strike against any object or structure within range. If the attack hits and the object isn't made of seastone, you can carve or remove up to a 5-foot square of space out of the material. The removed material is then moved out into an empty space within 5 feet of you.

**Spells (Cutting Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Snipping Hands (as Burning Hands, but dealing slashing damage instead; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Meld into Stone (3 charges), Stone Shape (4 charges), Wall of Stone (5 charges), or Passwall (5 cahrges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Spirit Thread Snip).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to perform a cutting technique that can sever even the threads of another creature's fighting spirit. Choose one creature you can see within 30 feet. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature's ties to one feature or ability, such as spellcasting or a special attack, are severed, rendering it unable to use that ability until it completes a long rest. On a successful save, the creature takes 6d6 force damage. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

\page


##### Pero Pero no Mi (Candy Creation)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Substance Generator Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A colorful striped spherical fruit with a very long stem on the bottom of it.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to create and manipulate candy at will. This candy can be used in various ways, from construction to combat, and has unique properties that allow it to be both hard as steel or soft and sticky.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Candy Creation.** You can create objects, weapons, or structures made of candy. These objects have a hardness and weight similar to steel but can be shaped and colored as you desire. As an action, you can create a candy object of a size up to a 5-foot cube. The object lasts for 1 hour or until you dismiss it.

**Sweet Combat.** Weapons you create from candy have the same properties as their normal counterparts but are considered magical for the purpose of overcoming resistance. You are proficient with any candy weapon you create.

**Candy Petrification.** As an action, you can spend 5 devil fruit charges to attempt to petrify a creature within 30 feet of you, turning them into candy. The target must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature is affected by the Flesh to Stone spell and has one failure. On a success, the creature isn't affected.

**Spells (Candy Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Candy Slug (Tenser's Floating Disk; 1 charge), Candy Armor (Mage Armor; 1 charge), Candy Net (Web; 2 charges), Candy Arrows (Cordon of Arrows; 2 charges), Candy Tentacles (Evard's Black Tentacles; 4 charges), or Wall of Candy (Wall of Stone; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Candy Gallery).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cover everyone within 60 feet of you with an extremely sticky and hardening candy. Each creature of your choice in the area must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, the target is restrained. It must then make a Constitution saving throw at the end of each of its turns. If it successfully saves three times, the spell ends. If it fails its save three times, it permanently turns to stone and is subjected to the petrified condition. The successes and failures don’t need to be consecutive; keep track of both until the target collects three of a kind. You can't use this feature again for another 24 hours.



```
```


##### Doru Doru no Mi (Wax)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Substance Generator Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A long cylindrical pale yellow fruit, with dripping patterns.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to create and manipulate wax, using it to form structures, weapons, and barriers. The wax is as hard as steel and can be shaped into nearly any form.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Wax Creation.** You can create objects, weapons, or structures made of wax. These objects have a hardness similar to steel but can be molded into complex shapes. As an action, you can create a wax object of a size up to a 5-foot cube. The object lasts for 1 hour or until you dismiss it.

**Wax Combat.** Weapons you create from wax have the same properties as their normal counterparts but are considered magical for the purpose of overcoming resistance. You are proficient with any wax weapon you create.

**Wax Petrification.** As an action, you can spend 5 devil fruit charges to attempt to petrify a creature within 30 feet of you, turning them into wax. The target must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature is affected by the Flesh to Stone spell and has one failure. On a success, the creature isn't affected.

**Spells (Wax Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Wax Armor (Mage Armor; 1 charge), Wax Bind (Hold Person; 2 charges), Wax Clones (Mirror Image; 2 charges), Control Wax (as Control Water but melting and controlling your wax instead of water; 4 charges), Wall of Wax (Wall of Stone; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Wax Sculptor).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to create a lifelike wax duplicate of an allied humanoid you can see within 60 feet. The duplicate acts as a Simulacrum with half the hit points of the original creature and follows your commands. The duplicate lasts for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

\page


##### Bomu Bomu no Mi (Bomb)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A round, pink fruit with a stem that resembles a fuse, and spiral patterns across its surface.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to create and detonate explosions at will. The user can also infuse parts of their body with explosive energy.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Explosion Immunity** You gain immunity to fire damage.

**Bomb Body.** Your body becomes highly explosive. When you are hit with a melee attack, you can use your reaction to cause an explosion, forcing the attacker to make a Dexterity saving throw (DC equal to your Devil Fruit save DC). On a failed save, they take 2d8 fire damage, or half as much damage on a successful one.

**Explosive Creation.** You can flick your explosive boogers You learn the fire bolt cantrip. Additionally, you can touch an object no larger than a 5-foot square and imbue it with explosive energy as an action. As a bonus action, you can cause the object to explode if it is within 60 feet of you. Any creature within a 10-foot radius must make a Dexterity saving throw (DC as above), taking 3d8 fire damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one. Only a number of objects equal to your proficiency bonus can remain explosive at a time, and it can only remain explosive in this way for 1 hour.

**Spells (Explosive Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Bombing Hands (Burning Hands; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Explosive Impact (shatter; 2 charges), Bomb Ball (fireball; 3 charges), Explosion Wall (wall of fire; 4 charges), and Flame Strike (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Final Detonation).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Delayed Blast Fireball, without expending a spell slot or material components. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.




```
```


##### Baku Baku no Mi (Munching)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A square-shaped fruit, similar in appearance to a die, with a blue-purple color and spiral patterns on its faces.

**Description.** Allows the user to eat virtually anything and everything, including inorganic substances, without harm to their body. Additionally, the user can gain the properties of anything they consume.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Anything Eater.** You can consume any material, including metal, wood, and stone, without suffering harm and it counts as food for you. Your teeth are also a natural weapon, which you can use to make unarmed strikes. If you hit with it, you deal bludgeoning damage equal to 1d10 + your Strength modifier.

**Gained Properties.** As an action you can make one unarmed strike against a material with your teeth. If it hits, you consume up to a 5-foot square of that material and you gain certain properties associated with it. Based on the material you eat, you gain the following features for 1 hour after consuming it (you can only gain one of these benefits at a time):

- **Cloth, Paper, or Rope.** your body becomes as light as paper. You have advantage on dexterity saves.

- **Glass, Crystal, or Ice.** your body becomes transparent and you gain advanctage on dexterity (stealth) checks.

- **Wood.** your skin has a bark-like appearance, and your AC can’t be less than 16, regardless of what kind of armor you are wearing. You can also use the thorn whip cantrip for the duration.

- **Stone.** your body becomes as hard as stone. You have resistance to nonmagical bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing damage.

- **Metal.** your skin has a tough, metallic appearance, and your AC can’t be less than 18, regardless of what kind of armor you are wearing.


**Spells (Munch Forms).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Regenerative Munch (Cure Wounds; Self; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Gecko Munch (spider climb; 2 charges), Air Bite (gaseous form; 3 charges), Form-Stealing Munch (polymorph spell into creature you've bitten within last hour; Self; 4 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Ultimate Munch Form).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast true polymorph, turning yourself into a creature you've bitten before, without expending a spell slot or material components. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

\page


##### Ato Ato no Mi (Art)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Altering Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A peach-shaped fruit with a purple top and a light orange bottom, with spiral patterns marking the division between the two colors.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to transform anything they touch into art and render it useless. This art can take any form the user imagines, so long as it vaguely resembles its previous form.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Art Transformation.** You can transform any inanimate, nonmagical object you can see into your own artistic interpretation of it. By spending 1 minute transforming an object no larger than 100 x 100 feet in size into a piece of art resembling its old form, you can render it useless in function for up to 10 hours. For example, if it is a ship or vehicle it can no longer take any actions to move. If it is a weapon or cannon, it can no longer be used to attack.

**Creature painting.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to target a creature within 30 feet of you. The creature must make a Wisdom saving throw against you Devil Fruit save DC or become incapacitated for 1 minute as it is transformed into a functionless piece of art. At the end of each of its turns, the target can make another Wisdom saving throw. On a success, the effect ends on the target.

**Spells (Art Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Sketch Mirage (Silent Image; 1 charge), Illusion Painting (Phantasmal Force; 2 charges), Materpiece Illusion (Major Image; 3 charges), Art Swirl (Hypnotic Pattern; 3 charges), Land of Art (Hallucinatory Terrain; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Art Dimension).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Demiplane, creating a demiplane full of art, without expending a spell slot or material components. Once you use this feature, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.



```
```


##### Beta Beta no Mi (Sticky Substance)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Substance Generator Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A yellow fruit, reminiscent of a lumpy pear, covered in a pattern of sticky swirls.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to generate and control a sticky substance. This substance can be used for a variety of purposes, from ensnaring enemies to climbing walls.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Sticky Substance Production.** You can generate a sticky substance from your body. As an action, you can cover a surface within 5 feet of you in this substance. An area covered in this substance is considered difficult terrain, and a creature that steps on or touches the sticky surface must succeed on a Strength (Athletics) check against your Devil Fruit save DC or be restrained until they succeed on the check. Objects that aren't being worn or carried will naturally stick and adhere to this substance. This coating lasts for 1 hour, and you can only cover up to 100 x 100 feet of a surface with this substance at once.

**Adhesive Travel.** You can use your sticky substance to stick to and climb vertical surfaces and ceilings without needing to make an ability check.

**Sticky Trap.** As an action, you can generate a large glob of sticky substance and fling it at a point you can see within 30 feet of you. Each creature in a 10-foot-radius sphere centered on that point must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or be restrained by the sticky substance. A creature restrained by the sticky substance can use its action to make a Strength check against your spell save DC. On a success, it is no longer restrained.

**Spells (Sticky Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Sticky Ground (entangle; 1 charge), Sticky Net (web; 2 charges), Sticky Bind (slow; 3 charges), Sticky Tentacles (Evard's Black Tentacles; 4 charges), Gorilla Glue (hold monster, 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Maximum Adherence).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cover everyone within 60 feet of you with an extremely sticky and hardening substance. Each creature of your choice in the area must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, the target is restrained. It must then make a Constitution saving throw at the end of each of its turns. If it successfully saves three times, the spell ends. If it fails its save three times, it permanently turns to stone and is subjected to the petrified condition. The successes and failures don’t need to be consecutive; keep track of both until the target collects three of a kind. You can't use this feature again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

\page


##### Buku Buku no Mi (Book)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A violet fruit with numerous ridges, covered in typical spiral patterns.

**Description.** Gives the user the ability to generate and manipulate books. Anything depicted or written within these books can be brought to reality or stored away, creating a powerful connection between the realms of fiction and reality.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Book Creation.** You can create books out of thin air, these books can be about any subject you have knowledge of. As an action, you can generate a book about a particular subject, granting you advantage on an Intelligence check related to that subject when you consult the book as part of the check.

**Fictional Manifestation.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charges to create a book that depicts a creature or an object, then turn a page to make it manifest in the real world for up to 1 hour. You must maintain concentration on this power to keep it (like concentration on a spell), or else the creature will return to your book. This can create simple objects no larger than huge or non-hostile, non-magical beasts (like horses, dogs, etc.) with a CR no greater than 1. The created creatures are friendly to you and your companions and follow simple commands.

**Spells (Book Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Hovering Books (Tenser's Floating Disk; 1 charge), Psychological Scroll (Detect Thoughts; 2 charges), Find Steed (2 charges), Conjure Animals (3 charges), World of Books (Hypnotic Pattern; 3 charges), Book Absorption (Banishment into a book; 4 charges), Find Greater Steed (4 charges), Conjure Elemental (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Library of Legends).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to create a grand book that brings a more powerful creature from its pages. You can summon any creature you've seen before with a CR no greater than 5. The summoned creature is friendly to you and obeys your commands. It disappears after 1 hour or when it drops to 0 hit points. Once you use this feature, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.



```
```


##### Example: Nuke Nuke no Mi (Phasing)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

	
**Fruit appearance.** Translucent purple apple with blue stripes
	
**Description.** Allows its user to phase through physical objects and forces physical projectiles and weapons to pass through the user as well.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Weapon Immunity.** You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through you. However, attacks made of living tissue do not phase through you, meaning you are not immune to unarmed strikes for example.
	
**Phase Movement.** You can choose to pass through physical objects as if they were difficult terrain, similar to a specter's incorporeal movement. However, this feature does not allow you to pass through living creatures. You take 5 (1d10) force damage if you end your turn inside an object.
	
Additionally, you can choose to allow any creature or object you are touching or grappling to share this feature with you so long as they are touching you.

**Spells.** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. Using your ability to phase through nonliving materials at rapid speeds and reappear somewhere else, you can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Absorb Elements (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Misty Step (2 charges), Blink (3 charges), Passwall (5 charges), Far Step (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Reality Phase).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Etherealness. You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Giro Giro no Mi (Insight)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A light pink, peach-shaped fruit with a curled stem and several swirly patterns across its surface.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to see through everything and read the thoughts and memories of others. It also allows the user to project their vision in the form of floating eyes that can see far distances and through solid objects.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**X-Ray Vision.** You gain the ability to see through solid objects. As an action, you can activate this vision, allowing you to see through up to 5 feet of wood, dirt, or stone, 1 foot of metal, or any amount of flesh or similar materials.

**Memory Peering.** You have advantage on insight checks. Additionally, as an action, you can read the surface thoughts of one creature within 30 feet of you. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or you gain insight into its reasoning (if any), its emotional state, and something that looms large in its mind (such as something it worries over, loves, or hates). Alternatively, you can use telepathy within 30 feet of you to transfer your memories or thoughts to another creature.

**Spells (Insight Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Detect Thoughts ( 2 charges), Tear Animals (conjure animals; 3 charges), Clairvoyance (3 charges), Arcane Eye (4 charges), Scrying (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Mind Pillage).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to delve deeper into a creature's mind, revealing its deepest secrets. The target must make a Wisdom saving throw against your spell save DC. On a failure, the target takes 6d10 psychic damage if you choose, and you gain information about its stats, true name, thoughts, history, identity, and background. On a success, the creature takes half as much psychic damage and you only identify its true name and surface thoughts. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

```


##### Gocha Gocha no Mi (Combining)

*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A red apple with swirl patterns covering its surface.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to merge with different living things or objects, enhancing their size and strength. The user can also incorporate the properties or abilities of the fused entity.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Fusion Enhancement.** As an action, you can merge with another willing creature or an object you touch. For 1 hour, your size category increases by one (up to a maximum of Gargantuan), and you gain advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. Your melee weapon attacks deal an extra 1d4 damage. You can only merge with one creature at a time using this ability. You can unmerge as a bonus action.

**Incorporate Properties.** When you merge with a creature or object, you can choose one of its properties or abilities to gain for the duration of the merge (subject to DM's discretion).

**Spells (Fusion Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Enlarge/Reduce (1 charge), Jump (2 charges), Longstrider (2 charges), Enhance Ability (2 charges), Stoneskin (Self; 4 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Grand Fusion).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to merge with up to three willing creatures or objects at the same time for 1 hour. Your size category increases by three (up to a maximum of Gargantuan), you gain advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws, and your melee weapon attacks deal an extra 3d4 damage. You can choose one property or ability from each fused entity to gain for the duration of the merge. Once you use this feature, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.



CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

\page


##### Hana Hana no Mi (Flower Blooming)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A light pink fruit covered with petal patterns.

**Description.** This fruit gives the user the ability to sprout parts of their body (usually hands or feet) on the surfaces of objects and living beings.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Limb Sprouting.** As an action, you can cause parts of your body to sprout on the surfaces of objects or living beings within 30 feet, for 1 minute. You can see, hear, and speak through these body parts as if you were in their place. These limbs share your AC and hit points, and can be attacked.

**Multi-Limb Actions.** As a bonus action, you can make an unarmed strike or attempt to grapple a creature within 30 feet using each sprouted limb (each limb gets an individual action). The attack uses your attack modifier and deals damage equal to an unarmed strike. If you grapple a creature with this ability, they are also restrained until the grapple is broken.

**Spells (Petal Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Arms of Hadar (1 charge), Arm Web (web; 2 charges), Hold Person (2 charges), Evard's Black Tentacles (4 charges), Bigby's Hand (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Demonio Fleur & Gran Jacuzzi Clutch).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to invoke the Demonio Fleur. You sprout a gargantuan, demonic avatar of your upper body within 60 feet. This avatar reflects your current hit points and your base AC (without armor), and shares your stats, resistances, immunities, and vulnerabilities. It does not have any equipment or weapons, it can't cast spells, and it acts on your initiative and its actions are controlled by you. It has a reach of 30 feet for its unarmed strikes, which deal damage equal to 2d8 + your strength modifier.

The sheer terror invoked by the Demonio Fleur forces all hostile creatures within 60 feet that can see it to make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or become frightened until the end of your next turn.

As a bonus action, you can command the Demonio Fleur to execute the Gran Jacuzzi Clutch. The Demonio uses its giant sprouted arms to grab a target within its reach. The target must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failure, they are restrained and take 6d10 bludgeoning damage; on a success, they take half damage and are not restrained.

The Demonio Fleur persists for 1 minute or until it drops to 0 hit points. Once you use this feature, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.

```


##### Hobi Hobi no Mi (Toy Transforming)

*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A cube-shaped, peach-like fruit with checkered patterns.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to transform living beings into toys by touching them. The user can also make a contract with the transformed toys, forcing them to obey their commands.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Toy Transformation.** As an action, you can touch a creature within 5 feet of you and force it to make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature is transformed into a toy version of itself, taking on the stats of a Monodrone (from the 5e monster manual). This transformation is permanent, unless removed by a Greater Restoration spell or a similar effect. Otherwise, its personality and mental ability scores remain the same. You can also determine its size (tiny to gargantuan). The creature also loses any ability to cast spells, and any special abilities it may have had in its original form. While in toy form, the creature is charmed by you and cannot harm you, and you can erase its memories while it is a toy. If you fall to 0 hit points, fall unconscious, or fall victim to your Sea Weakness, every creature under the effects of your Toy Transformation reverts back to their original form. Alternatively, a creature can be freed from this effect with the Greater Restoration or Wish spells. A creature that succeeds on saving against your Toy Transformation or is otherwise reverted back to its original form is immune to the effects of it for 24 hours.

**Contract Making.** As a bonus action, you can make a contract with a toy you have transformed. The toy obeys any verbal commands that you issue to it (no action required by you), as long as they don't involve harming you. If you are absent, the toy acts on its own to carry out your last given command.

**Spells (Toy Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Toy Servant (unseen servant; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Hold Toy (as hold person; only works on toys of any size; 2 charges), Summon Toy (summon construct; 4 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Overdrive Transformation).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cause all creatures within 30 feet of you to make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, they are transformed into toys, and are subject to the effects of your Toy Transformation and Contract Making abilities. Once you use this feature, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.

##### Horo Horo no Mi (Ghost)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Substance Generator Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A rounded, white fruit with a stem that spirals at the top, and multiple swirl patterns on its surface.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to create and control spectral entities known as "ghosts", manifesting various effects.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Astral Projection.** As an action, you can create a ghostly avatar from your body, resembling yourself. You can see through the ghost's senses, speak through it, and hear what it hears while it is within 1,000 feet of you. The entity acts according to your will and is immune to all damage types. It can fly up to 60 feet during your turn, and it can pass through walls, as if using the Incorporeal Movement feature, though it cannot pass through water or seastone. As an action, you can cause it to phase into the Ethereal Plane or back into the Material Plane. As an action, you can increase or decrease its size by one category. You can only have one ghostly avatar active at a time and it lasts until you fall unconscious or fall victim to your Sea Weakness.

**Negative Hollow.** As an action, you can summon a small hollow from yourself or your ghostly avatar to touch a creature within 30 feet of the source (you or your ghostly avatar). The creature must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or become affected by the ghost's negative energy, causing the target to fall into deep depression and lose the will to fight and become incapacitated for 1 minute. An affected creature can repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success and it becomes immune to your negative hollow for 24 hours.

**Spells (Ghost Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Cause Fear (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Hollow Detonation (shatter; 2 charges), Phantasmal Force (2 charges), Fear (3 charges), Confusion (4 charges), Phantasmal Killer (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Phantom Uprising).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to unleash a spectral maelstrom. Ghosts flood from you in a 60-foot radius and move through creatures and objects within the area. Each creature in the area must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be affected by the ghost’s negative energy, becoming frightened, and incapacitated with despair for 1 minute. An affected creature can repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success. Additionally, non-magical objects in the area are phased into the ethereal plane for the duration. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.






##### Horu Horu no Mi (Hormones)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Substance Generator Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A pink pineapple-shaped fruit with a curly stem, and several curly patterns around it.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to create and control various hormones, which can be used to modify the bodies and minds of other creatures.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Syringe Fingers.** Your needle-like fingers are a natural weapon, which you can use to make unarmed strikes. If you hit with it, you deal piercing damage equal to 1d6 + your Strength modifier, instead of the bludgeoning damage normal for an unarmed strike.

**Hormone Manipulation.** You can use an action to alter the hormones of one willing creature you touch. An unwilling creature must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. This can cause one of the following effects: change the target's sex, give the target advantage on checks made with Strength, Dexterity, or Constitution (pick one) for 1 minute, or alter the target's current emotional state.

**Life-Risking Operation.** As an action, you can touch a creature and expend 1 devil fruit charge to remove any one disease or neutralize one poison affecting it. The creature can also immediately end one effect on it that causes it to be charmed or frightened.

**Spells (Hormone Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Cure Wounds (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Enhance Ability (2 charges), Haste (3 charges), Greater Restoration (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Endocrine Dominance).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to release a powerful surge of hormones within a 60-foot radius centered on yourself. Enemy creatures in the area must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC, and friendly creatures can choose whether they are affected or not. On a failed save, creatures are subject to one of the following effects of your choice for 1 minute:
- Adrenaline Surge: The creature's speed doubles, and it gains advantage on Strength, Dexterity, or Constitution (choose one) checks and saving throws.
- Emotional Collapse: The creature becomes slowed (as if affected by the slow spell) with overwhelming emotions of sadness, fear, or joy.
- Physical Atrophy: The creature's Strength, Dexterity, or Constitution (choose one) checks and saving throws are made at disadvantage.

An affected creature can make a new Constitution saving throw at the end of each of its turns to end the effect early. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Hoya Hoya no Mi (Genie Lamp)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Substance Generator Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A turquoise fruit resembling a melon with various intricate swirl patterns and star-like designs.

**Description.** This devil fruit grants the user the ability to summon a genie-like entity from their body. This powerful spirit is bound to the user's will and aids them in combat.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Genie Manifestation.** As an action, you can summon the genie from within you by rubbing your body like a lamp. A Djinni genie (stat block for Djinni is in the standard 5e Monster Manual) appears in an unoccupied space you can see within 30 feet of you. The genie lacks its Innate Spellcasting ability and Elemental Demise, and has hit points equal to your own. It remains as long as you concentrate (as if concentrating on a spell), to a maximum of 12 hours, or until it drops to 0 hit points. It then returns into your body. 

While summoned, the djinni is friendly to you and your companions. It obeys any commands you give it. If you fail to command it, the djinni defends itself against attackers but takes no other actions. 

After the djinni departs, it can’t be summoned again until the next dawn. You can only have one genie summoned at a time.

**Spells (Genie Abilities).** The genie has a pool of 9 charges. It can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells without needing to expend material components: Thunderwave (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Detect Evil and Good (1 charge), Gust of Wind (2 charges), Invisibility (2 charges), Gaseous Form (3 charges), Wind Wall (3 charges), Major Image (3 charges), or Creation (5 charges). The genie regains expended charges when it is re-summoned.

**Awakening (Genie Unleashed).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to enhance your genie's power, turning it into a massive, even more formidable form. The genie's hit points double, its size increases to huge, its attacks deal an extra ammount equal to your proficiency bonus, and it radiates an aura in a 20-foot radius. Enemy creatures within the aura must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be frightened until the end of their next turn. This empowered state lasts for the duration of your Awakened state. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Ishi Ishi no Mi (Stone Control)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A rough-textured, grayish fruit resembling a boulder with jagged patterns on its surface.

**Description.** This devil fruit grants the user the ability to merge with, control, and reshape any form of stone they come into contact with. This allows for a versatile range of combat and defensive capabilities, as well as the ability to traverse through stone as if it were liquid.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Stone Meld.** As an action, you can merge with any stone surface, allowing you to traverse through it, effectively disappearing from sight. While merged, you can move within and emerge from any connected stone surface within 60 feet.

**Stone Manipulation.** You can reshape and control stone structures within 30 feet of you. This can be used to form weapons, barriers, or even simple tools. As an action, you can create a large-sized stone object (AC 17; with 27 (5d10) hit points). You can only do this once per minute.

**Stone Body.** You can spend 4 devil fruit charges to mold the stone around you to polymorph (as if using the polymorph spell) yourself into a stone construct or earth elemental that has a challenge rating equal to or less than your level for up to 1 hour. However, your mental ability scores remain the same and you can speak while in this form. You remain this way as long as you concentrate on maintaining it (as if concentrating on a spell). The transformation lasts for the duration, or until you drop to 0 hit points or die. You can continue to use your Devil Fruit abilities and spells in this form, so long as they don't require concentration, but cannot use any other class or racial features or spells for the duration.

**Spells (Stone Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Earth Tremor (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Maximilian’s Earthen Grasp (2 charges), Erupting Earth (3 charges), Stone Shape (4 charges), Stoneskin (4 charges), Wall of Stone (5 charges), Passwall (5 charges), or Transmute Rock (5 charges). You regain expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Terracotta Titan).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to pull from the very essence of the earth beneath you, creating a massive golem or suit of stone armor around yourself for 1 minute. In this state, you gain the benefits of your Stone Body devil fruit feature without needing to expend devil fruit charges, but can increase your size up to garganutan while polymorphed. You gain resistance to all damage (except force), your physical attacks deal additional damage equal to your proficiency bonus, and you have advantage on strength checks and saving throws. This empowered state lasts for 1 minute. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Noko Noko no Mi (Mushroom Spores)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Substance Generator Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A vibrant orange, bulbous fruit with white dot patterns.

**Description.** This devil fruit grants the user the ability to produce, control, and manipulate various mushroom spores with different properties, ranging from healing to poisoning. The user can cultivate these spores on any surface, living or non-living.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Poisonous Spores.** You become immune to poison damage and the poisoned condition. Additionally, you can cast the poison spray cantrip without expending any material components.

**Hallucination Spores.** As an action, you can eject spores at one creature you can see within 30 feet of you. The target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be poisoned for 1 minute. The poisoned target is incapacitated while it hallucinates. The target can repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on itself on a success and it becomes immune to your hallucination and pacifying spores for 24 hours.

**Pacifying Spores.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to eject spores at one creature you can see within 30 feet of you. The target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be stunned for 1 minute. The target can repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the condition on itself on a success and it becomes immune to your hallucination and pacifying spores for 24 hours.

**Spells (Spore Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Sleep (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Spore Barrage (as Cloud of Daggers but deals poison or acid damage; 2 charges), Stinking Cloud (3 charges), Spore Bomb (as Vitriolic Sphere; 4 charges), Cloudkill (5 charges). You regain expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Maximum Melting Spore Cloud).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Incendiary Cloud, without expending a spell slot or material components. It deals poison or acid damage (your choice) instead of fire damage. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.
