```


##### Kibi Kibi no Mi (Beast Control)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Substance Generator Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A bright yellow, rough-skinned fruit resembling a kiwi but with pronounced spikes protruding outwards.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to produce dango dumplings which allow them to command and control any beast which consumes it, allowing for communication, understanding, and allegiance with the beast.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Beast Command.** As an action, you can throw a dango at the mouth of a beast you can see within 30 feet of you by spending 1 Devil Fruit charge. The targeted beast must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC to avoid the Dango. On a failed save, the beast is under your command (as if using animal friendship) for 1 month. The beast must not be a Zoan user or an otherwise polymorphed creature. If the beast suffers harm from you or your allies, it can make a Wisdom saving throw, breaking free on a success.

**Beast regeneration.** Once per long rest, you heal a beast you control and can see within 30 feet of you with a dango. By spending 1 Devil Fruit charge, the beast regains one of its hit dice plus your proficiency bonus in hit points.

**Animal Empathy.** You gain advantage on all Wisdom (Insight) checks related to understanding beasts and their emotions.

**Spells (Beast Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Bless (targeting beasts you control; 1 charge), Enhance Ability (targeting a beast you control; 2 charges), Beast Bond (Warding Bond on a beast you control; 2 charges), Elemental Collar (Protection from Energy on a beast you control; 3 charges), Wild Surge (Haste on a beast you control; 3 charges), or Greater Restoration (targeting a beast you control; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Beast Master's Dominion).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to release an aura in a 120-foot radius. All beasts within this radius must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be brought under your command for 10 minutes. A targeted beast must not be a Zoan user or an otherwise polymorphed creature. If a controlled beast suffers harm from you or your allies, it can make another Wisdom saving throw, breaking free on a success. You can't use this feature again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA


\page






##### Kage Kage no Mi (Shadows)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A dark-purple, nearly black, heart-shaped fruit with spiraled patterns running from its stem to its base.

**Description.** Grants the user the ability to manipulate shadows, stealing them from living beings, and attaching them to other entities, including inanimate objects, thereby animating them.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Shadow Thief.** As an action, you can attempt to grab the shadow of a creature within 10 feet of you, so long as it has a CR of 1/8 or higher. The target must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or have its shadow stolen. A creature can retrieve its shadow by destroying an undead or object which holds its shadow, or by placing salt in its mouth (touch; athletics or Sleight of Hand against the undead or object's Athletics or Acrobatics), or by stealing it back from you if you are holding it (touch; athletics or Sleight of Hand against your Athletics or Acrobatics). A creature missing its shadow falls victim to a vampire's Sunlight Hypersensitivity weakness (5e Monster Manual). When you successfully steal a shadow from a creature, you gain 1 Devil Fruit charge. If a creature who has had its shadow stolen dies, you lose its shadow and thereby lose 1 devil fruit charge.

**Shadow Animate.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to animate a single medium or smaller sized dead creature or inanimate object (as if using animate dead or animate objects) by infusing it with a shadow you have stolen, except it has the same stats it would have if it were alive. A dead creature's CR must be equal to or less than 1 to be animated this way. This effect lasts until you end it as a bonus action (thus gaining 1 devil fruit charge as the shadow leaves its body) or it is destroyed (and the shadow returns to its host's body). If you wish to infuse a higher CR dead creature or larger object with shadows to animate it, you must spend a total number of charges equal to its CR (CR must be no greater than half your character level rounded up), or an additional charge for each size category the object is over medium, up to Huge (E.g. 2 charges for large, 3 for huge). 

**Shadow Asgard.** You can absorb stolen shadows into your body to become larger and more powerful. By spending 1 Devil Fruit charge, you absorb a shadow into yourself. For each shadow you absorb, you gain 10 temporary hit points (which only stacks with each additional shadow absorbed) up to a maximum of 30, your weapon attacks deal an extra 1d4 damage (up to a maximum bonus of 3d4), your reach with melee weapons extends by 5 feet (up to a 15 foot total bonus), and your size increases by one (up to gargantuan). While this form is active, you have advantage on strength checks and saving throws. When you lose all temporary hit points granted by this ability, the shadows are expelled from your body and returned to its original host, and this ability ends.

**Doppelman.** You can detach your own shadow and animate it as a bonus action in an unoccupied space you can see within 15 feet of you. This shadow is a magical, translucent, dark image of you that lasts until it is destroyed, until you dismiss it as a bonus action, until you manifest another shadow, or until you're incapacitated.

Your shadow has AC 14 + your proficiency bonus, 1 hit point, and immunity to all conditions and all damage except force and radiant damage. If it has to make a saving throw, it uses your saving throw bonus for the roll. It is the same size as you, and it occupies its space. On your turn, you can mentally command the shadow to move up to 30 feet in any direction (no action required). If your shadow is ever more than a mile away from you at the end of your turn, it is destroyed. If your Doppelman touches water or salt, it is also destroyed.

As a bonus action, you can teleport, magically swapping places with your shadow at a cost of 15 feet of your movement, regardless of the distance between the two of you.
When you take the Attack action on your turn, any attack you make with that action can originate from your space or the shadow's space. You make this choice for each attack.

When a creature that you can see within 5 feet of your shadow moves at least 5 feet away from it, you can use your reaction to make an opportunity attack against that creature as if you were in the shadow's space.

If your Doppelman is ever destroyed or dismissed, your shadow returns to you. While your shadow is missing, you also fall victim to the vampire's Sunlight Hypersensitivity weakness.

**Spells (Shadow Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 maximum charges, but you start with none. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components, with the source of the spell being yourself or your Doppelman: Shadow Arms (Arms of Hadar; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Darkness (2 charges), Shadow Blade (2 charges), Shadow Bat Barrage (Conjure Barrage; 3 charges), Evard's Black Tentacles (4 charges), Night Parade (Danse Macabre or Animate Objects; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges when shadows are collected from Shadow Thief.

**Awakening (Shadow Legion).** Once you've awakened your power, you can pull shadows from all objects around you and use an action to conjure up to 10 Shadows (see the Monster Manual for statistics), for up to 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. The Shadows form in unoccupied spaces within 100 feet of you and obey your commands for 1 minute or until they are destroyed. You can dismiss one shadow as a free action during your turn, once per turn, and animate a dead creature you can see within 60 feet of you. The target rises at the start of your next turn as a zombie that is under your command for the duration of your awakening, following your verbal orders to the best of its ability. Once you use ability, you can't use it again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA



\page



##### Kiro Kiro no Mi (Kilogram)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A heavy, light red-colored cylindrical apple with a sturdy stem and swirls across its surface.

**Description.** This fruit grants the user the ability to manipulate their weight without changing their size. At will, the user can become as light as a feather or as heavy as a ton, granting them significant advantages in combat and mobility.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Weight Manipulation.** As an action, you can adjust your weight to 1 gram or 10,000 kilograms (10 metric tons) for 1 minute, or return to your regular weight. Changing your weight does not change your physical size or shape, and you return to your normal weight if you are knocked unconscious.

- __When you weigh 1 gram:__ Your movement speed doubles, you can move over water or fragile surfaces without breaking them, you don't take fall damage, and you make dexterity checks and saving throws at advantage but make strength checks and saving throws at disadvantage. Your jump distance is also tripled.
- __When you weigh 10,000 kilograms:__ Your melee attacks deal an extra 2d8 bludgeoning damage, your speed and jump distance is halved, and you make strength checks and saving throws at advantage but make dexterity checks and saving throws at disadvantage. You are also immune to being pushed or pulled against your will.

**Gravity Slam.** When you're in the air (such as from a jump or fall), as a part of your action to become 10,000 kilograms, you can also deliver a crushing blow to enemies below you. All creatures within a 10-foot radius from where you land must make a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (their choice) against your Devil Fruit save DC or take 4d10 bludgeoning damage and be knocked prone. If they succeed, they take half damage and aren't knocked prone. You do not take fall damage so long as you don't fall more than 30 feet as a part of this ability.

**Spells (Kilogram Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Earth Tremor (while 10,000 kilograms; Self; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Misty Step (while 1 gram; 2 charges), Erupting Earth (while 10,000 kilograms; Self; Doesn't affect you; 3 charges), Levitate (while 1 gram; Self; 3 charges), Destructive Wave (while 10,000 kilograms; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Absolute Gravity).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Gravity Fissure at the 7th level, without expending a spell slot or material components. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

```




##### Kobu Kobu no Mi (Encourage)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A deep red, heart-shaped fruit with gold streaks across its surface resembling cheering hands.

**Description.** This fruit grants the user the ability to bolster and encourage allies, enhancing their abilities and healing their wounds through sheer willpower and motivation.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Encouraged Human.** You learn the guidance cantrip. Additionally, you are immune to being frightened and have advantage on saving throws against any effect that would discourage you from fighting. You have advantage on any Charisma (Persuasion) check made to encourage a creature.

**Aura of Encouragement.** Whenever you or a friendly creature within 10 feet of you make an ability check, attack roll, or saving throw, the creature adds a +2 bonus to the roll. Additionally, creatures in this range cannot be frightened while you are conscious. You can spend 1 devil fruit charge to extend this radius up to 30 feet for 1 minute.

**Spells (Encourage Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Heroism (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Aid (2 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Beacon of Hope (3 charges), Motivational Speech (3 charges), Aura of Life (4 charges), Mass Cure Wounds (5 charges), or Circle of Power (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Unyielding Aura).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Holy Aura, without expending a spell slot or material components. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Memo Memo no Mi (Memory Control)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A pale lavender fruit, shaped like an intricate brain, with coiling patterns reminiscent of neurons and synaptic connections.

**Description.** This devil fruit grants the user the power to manipulate, alter, and even erase the memories of those they touch. It can also allow the user to implant false memories or even transfer memories from one individual to another.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Memory Thread.** As an action, you can touch a willing creature or unwilling creature and force it to make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failure or if the creature allows you, you can pull out film strips from the creature's head to view their memories for 1 minute. While the film strip is pulled out of the creature's head, it is incapacitated for the duration. Each time the creature takes damage in this state, it can make an additional Wisdom saving throw at advantage to break free. You can edit the creature's memory film in the following ways while it is removed:

- **Memory Alteration:** As an action, while touching the creature, you can modify or erase parts of its memories. This alteration is permanent unless reversed by you or a spell like Greater Restoration.

- **Memory Implantation:** As an action, while touching the creature, you can implant a false memory into it. It will remember the false memory as if it really happened.

**Spells (Memory Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Bad Memory Threads (Bane; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Memory Flood (Hold Person; 2 charges), Detect Thoughts (2 charges), Zone of Truth (2 charges), Memory Mail (Sending; 3 charges), Dream (4 charges), Modify Memory (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Destructive Memory Blast).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to flood enemies in the area with bad memories by casting Psychic Scream, without expending a spell slot or material components. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

```


##### Mero Mero no Mi (Love)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A pink, heart-shaped fruit adorned with a multitude of arrow-like patterns.

**Description.** This fruit grants the user the power to turn anyone who feels lust or attraction towards them into stone. 

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Petrifying Gaze.** As an action, you can meet the gaze of a creature within 30 feet. If that creature has ever felt any form of attraction or lust toward you, it must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature is affected by the Flesh to Stone spell, and has one failure. If the creature avoids looking into your eyes (such as by averting their gaze or closing their eyes), they have advantage on the saving throw. Once a creature saves, it is immune to the effects of your Petrifying Gaze for 24 hours. Creatures that are incapable of feeling attraction or lust, such as by being immune to the charmed condition, are also immune to this effect. You can end this petrification on a creature at will.

**Love Beam.** As an action, you can spend 3 devil fruit charges to shoot a 30-foot cone of magical attraction from your hands. Each creature in this cone must make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failed save, they are charmed with feelings of attraction and lust for 1 minute. While charmed in this way, they will move toward you and assist you during their turn and you can use a bonus action to use your petrifying gaze on one of the charmed creatures, even if they hadn’t felt attraction toward you before. If the creature ends its turn in a location where it doesn’t have line of sight to you or takes damage, the creature can make a Wisdom saving throw. On a successful save, the effect ends for that creature. Once a creature saves, it is immune to the effects of your Love Beam for 24 hours.

**Spells (Love Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Charm Person (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Enthrall (2 charges), Hold Person (2 charges), Compulsion (4 charges), Dominate Person (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Love Arrow Storm).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to blast everyone within 60 feet of you with a barrage of love arrows. Each creature in the area must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, the target is charmed by you. It must then make a Wisdom saving throw at the end of each of its turns while charmed this way. If it successfully saves three times, the effect ends. If it fails its save three times, it permanently turns to stone and is subjected to the petrified condition. The successes and failures don’t need to be consecutive; keep track of both until the target collects three of a kind. You can't use this feature again for another 24 hours.

##### Mira Mira No Mi (Mirror)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** The Mira Mira no Mi looks like a shiny, silver apple, its surface perfectly reflective. The texture is smooth and cold to the touch, much like glass.

**Description.** The Mira Mira no Mi gifts its user the power to create and manipulate mirrors, as well as to use reflective surfaces as portals. The user becomes a "Mirror Human."

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Mirror Surface.** With a touch, you can transform any surface, no larger than a 10-foot square, into a mirror for up to 1 hour.

**Mirror Portal.** As an action, you can turn a mirror you touch into a portal to the mirror dimension until the start of your next turn. Any creature which enters the mirror is brought into the mirror dimension, similar to the Demiplane spell. The mirror dimension connects all nearby mirrors, allowing you to exit out of a mirror connected to the dimension. You can speak to the mirrors in this dimension, as they are sentient, asking them questions they would understand and know. These can be questions about creatures the mirror has seen, where a specific mirror leads to, or where specific mirrors are located in the dimension.

The DM determines the size, shape, and terrain within the mirror dimension. A creature cannot enter or leave the mirror dimension unless a mirror portal is specifically activated by you.

**Reflective Defense.** When hit by a melee attack, you can use your reaction and spend 5 devil fruit charges to create a mirror shield, causing the damage to become 0. The attacker must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the attacker takes half of the damage they would have dealt to you, as the attack is redirected back to them.

**Spells (Reflective Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Disguise Self (1 charge), Silent Image (1 charge), Mirror Image (2 charges), Phantasmal Force (2 charges), Major Image (3 charges), Hallucinatory Terrain (4 charges), Phantasmal Killer (4 charges), Mislead (5 charges), Seeming (5 charges), and Scrying (using a mirror as a focus; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Mirror Prison).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast the Maze spell, no spells slots or material components required. The target is sucked into the mirror dimension and trapped there temporarily. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Modo Modo no Mi (Reduce Age)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** An emerald green fruit resembling an hourglass, with swirling patterns on its surface.

**Description.** This devil fruit bestows upon its user the unique ability to turn back the hands of time, reversing the age of creatures or even inanimate objects by 12 years.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Age Reversal (Creatures).** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to toss an orb of energy at a creature or Huge or smaller object within 30 feet of you, reducing its age by 12 years. If the target is unwilling to have its age reversed, it can make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a success, its age remains the same. This change affects the physical age only, not the creature's memories, mental maturity, or experiences. If a creature is reduced down from an adult to a child, it will have disadvantage on attack rolls, ability checks, and saving throws until its age is reverted by a Greater Restoration spell or a similar effect, or if you choose to end the effect. Every creature and object that has been affected by this ability will be also be returned to its original age if you are knocked unconscious, thus ending this effect on them. If a creature is reduced down to below 0 years in age, it is erased from exiistence.

**Object Restoration.** As an action, you can touch an inanimate object that is no larger than Huge and reverse its age, potentially repairing wear and tear or damage it has sustained over the years. This can be used to restore a broken item, undo the effects of time on a painting, or return a rusted weapon to its prime state. The object remains in its restored state permanently unless physically damaged again. An object that may have existed in a previous state of matter, such as volcanic rock, may be returned to its previous state (which would be lava) with this ability.

**Spells (Precise Reversal).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Wound Reversal (Cure Wounds; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Lesser Restoration (2 charges), Reverse Death (Revivify; 3 charges), Fabricate (4 charges), Greater Reverse Death (Raise Dead; 5 charges), Passwall (5 charges), or Greater Restoration (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Maximum Reversal).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Time Ravage, no spells slots or material components required. However, you instead reverse a creature's age to 30 days after it is born on a failed save, and its size becomes tiny. If the targeted creature is exactly 12 years old or less, it is instantly erased from existence on a failed save. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Netsu Netsu no Mi (Heat)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A deep-red fruit resembling a chili pepper with small flame-like patterns scattered over its skin.

**Description.** This devil fruit grants its user the ability to generate intense heat from their body, allowing them to raise the temperature of objects they touch or emit scorching waves of heat around them.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Burning Touch.** You learn the Shocking Grasp cantrip, but deal fire damage with it instead of lightning. Additionally, you are immune to fire damage.

**Heat Emission.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to emit a wave of heat in a 15-foot radius around you. Creatures in this area must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, creatures take 3d6 fire damage, and half as much on a success. The heat ignites any flammable objects in the area that aren’t being worn or carried.

**Heat Armor.** As a bonus action, for up to 1 hour or until you fall unconscious, you can raise the temperature of your body to such an extent that any creature making a melee attack against you and hits within 5 feet takes 1d6 fire damage. A creature which touches you or starts its turn in contact with you also takes 1d6 fire damage. You can end this effect early as a bonus action.

**Spells (Heat Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Searing Smite (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Heat Metal (2 charges), Flame Blade (2 charges), Fire Shield (warm shield only; 4 charges), Immolation (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Inferno Emanation).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Fire Storm, without expending a spell slot or material components. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Frizu Frizu no Mi (Cold)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A pale blue fruit with white swirl patterns.

**Description.** This devil fruit empowers its user to generate intense cold, allowing them to lower the temperature of objects they touch, emit chilling waves of cold around them, and even freeze liquids on contact.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Chilling Touch.** You learn the Frostbite cantrip. Additionally, you are immune to cold damage.

**Cold Emission.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to emit a wave of biting frost in a 15-foot radius around you. Creatures in this area must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, creatures take 3d6 cold damage, and half as much on a success. The cold freezes any liquid in the area.

**Frostbite Armor.** As a bonus action, for up to 1 hour or until you fall unconscious, you can lower the temperature of your body to such an extent that any creature making a melee attack against you and hits within 5 feet takes 1d6 cold damage. A creature which touches you or starts its turn in contact with you also takes 1d6 cold damage. You can end this effect early as a bonus action.

**Spells (Cold Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Frost Fingers (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Rime's Binding Ice (2 charges), Sleet Storm (3 charges), Ice Storm (4 charges), Fire Shield (chill shield only; 4 charges), Cone of Cold (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Blizzard Emanation).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Freezing Sphere at the 7th level, without expending a spell slot or material components. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Noro Noro no Mi (Slow)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A golden, translucent fruit with a slightly reflective surface, resembling a shimmering crystal orb.

**Description.** This devil fruit grants its user the unique power to emit "Noro Noro" beams, which can slow down any object or creature they touch, making them experience time at a drastically reduced speed.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Slow Immunity.** You cannot be slowed by any means, such as by the Slow spell or by a Stone Golem.

**Slowing Shot.** As an action, you can target a creature, or a Large or smaller object, within 30 feet with a miniature slowing beam. A creature must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature is slowed, as if affected by the Slow spell for 1 minute. A creature affected by this ability makes another Wisdom saving throw at the end each of its turns. On a successful save, the effect ends for it. An object targeted by this ability remains nearly frozen in place for the duration, only moving 5 feet per turn if it was in motion. 

**Slowing Beam.** As an action, you can spend 3 devil fruit charges to shoot a 30-foot cone of slowing energy from your hands. Each creature in this cone must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, they are affected by the Slow spell for 30 seconds. A creature affected by this ability makes another Wisdom saving throw at the end each of its turns. On a successful save, the effect ends for it. Any objects in this cone remain nearly frozen in place for the duration, only moving 5 feet per turn if it was in motion. You do not need to concentrate to keep a creature slowed in this way.

**Spells (Slow Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Hold Person (2 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Slow (3 charges), Temporal Shunt (5 charges), or Hold Monster (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Temporal Lockdown).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Time Stop, without expending a spell slot or material components, as the world around you slows to a halt. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Ori Ori no Mi (Cage)

*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Substance Producer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A silvery fruit, resembling a chain wrapped in a tight ball with small links and padlock motifs imprinted on its surface.

**Description.** This devil fruit bestows upon its user the ability to generate and manipulate iron shackles and cages. With a mere gesture or touch, the user can bind or imprison their foes, making escape incredibly difficult.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Chain Whip.** You learn the thorn whip cantrip, no material components required. It deals bludgeoning damage instead of piercing, and appears as steel chains.

**Shackling Touch.** As an action, you can touch a creature within 5 feet. The target must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature is bound by iron shackles, becoming restrained until it can break free. A creature can use its action to make a Strength check against your Devil Fruit save DC, breaking free on a success.

**Cage Conjuring.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to conjure a cage around one creature you can see within 30 feet. The target must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature is trapped inside the cage, which has an AC of 20 and 30 hit points. The bars are spaced far too narrowly for creatures or weapons to fit through, giving it full cover. The cage lasts for up to 1 minute, after which it disappears.

**Spells (Cage Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Entangle (1 charge), Hold Person (2 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Web (reskinned as chains instead of webs; not flammable; 2 charges), Dimension Cage (Banishment; 4 charges), Wall of Force (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Prison Realm).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to manifest a large prison complex in a 30-foot radius sphere centered on a point you can see within 60 feet. Within this area, iron walls and cages transforming the terrain into a labyrinthine jail. Creatures in the area must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, they are trapped within individual cages, becoming restrained. A creature can break free by making a Strength check against your Devil Fruit save DC. If a creature is freed, it must also spend an action to make a DC 20 Intelligence check to find the exit within the labyrinth prison, at which point it appears 5 feet outside of the prison complex in an area it chooses. The prison lasts for 10 minutes or until you fall unconscious, after which it disappears. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Oshi Oshi no Mi (Pushing)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A dark brown, almost earthen-colored fruit with undulating ridges on its surface, reminiscent of clay.

**Description.** This devil fruit bestows its user with the unprecedented ability to alter and mold the very ground beneath their feet. They can push, pull, or shape terrain as if it were soft clay, creating structures or modifying the landscape to their whims.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Enhanced Pushing.** When you use an action to shove a creature, you gain advantage on your Strength (Athletics) check. If you choose to push a creature away, you can choose to push it up to 15 feet away from you instead.

**Tunnel Pushing.** You gain a burrowing speed of 30 feet. You can burrow through solid rock at half your burrow speed and leave a 5-foot-diameter tunnel in your wake. As an action, you can reshape a 10-foot cube of earth or stone you can touch within 5 feet. You can form it into any shape that suits your purpose: creating ramps, walls, pits, or any other structure. The reshaped terrain has the durability of its original material.

**Ground Wave.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to create a wave-like ripple on the ground in a 15-foot wide line that's 60 feet long. Each creature standing on the ground in that area must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or take 1d6 bludgeoning damage and be knocked prone. If the ground in that area is loose earth or stone, it becomes difficult terrain until cleared.

**Spells (Pushing Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Earth Tremor (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Maximillian's Earthen Grasp (2 charges), Erupting Earth (3 charges), Wall of Stone (5 charges), Passwall (5 charges), or Transmute Rock (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Infinite Tunnel).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to exert total control over the ground to form a 10-foot magical tunnel in the earth leading to one location you're aware of. After you create the tunnel, any creature that jumps into it teleports to a location of your choosing, as if using the Teleport spell (there can only be one target destination). The destination must be known to you, it must be connected to the earth, and it must be on the same plane of existence. The tunnel lasts for 1 minute, then collapses and disappears. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

```




##### Oto Oto no Mi (Sound)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A vibrant orange fruit, resembling a bell with multiple musical note motifs across its surface.

**Description.** This devil fruit grants the user the capability to manifest musical instruments from their body. Using these instruments, they can produce sound waves that can have a range of effects, from disorienting enemies to causing physical harm.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Sound Immunity.** You are immune to thunder damage and the deafened condition.

**Instrumental Manifestation.** As a bonus action, you can generate any musical instrument from your body, from flutes to drums to guitars. When you produce an instrument, you are proficient with it and can immediately play it. You must use this as the focus for your Devil Fruit spells and abilities.

**Dissonant Blast.** You learn the thunderclap cantrip. Additionally, as an action while holding an instrument you've manifested, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to play a harsh note that emits a blast of disruptive sound. Each creature in a 30-foot cone originating from you must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC, taking 3d8 thunder damage on a failed save or half as much damage on a successful one. A creature that is immune to the deafened condition is not affected by this ability.

**Spells (Sound Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Thunderwave (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Shatter (2 charges), Hypnotic Pattern (reskinned as a captivating melody; 3 charges), Destructive Wave (thunder damage only; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Orchestra of Doom).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to manifest an orchestra of instruments around you. For the next minute or until you fall unconscious, these instruments play a haunting and overpowering symphony. Each creature of your choice within a 60-foot radius of you must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC at the start of each of their turns or take 7d8 thunder damage, half as much on a success. A creature that is immune to the deafened condition cannot be affected by this ability. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Sabi Sabi no Mi (Rusting)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A maroon fruit with a rough texture, resembling corroded metal with flaky patches and rust-like patterns.

**Description.** This devil fruit gives its user the uncanny ability to induce rapid rusting and decay in metals. With just a touch or gesture, the user can make the sturdiest of metals brittle and fragile.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Rust Body.** Any weapon made of metal that hits you corrodes. After dealing damage, the weapon takes a permanent and cumulative -1 penalty to damage rolls. If its penalty drops to -5, the weapon is destroyed. Ammunition made of metal that hits you is destroyed after dealing damage.

**Corroding Touch.** You corrode a ferrous metal object you can see within 5 feet of you. If the object isn't being worn or carried, the touch destroys a 1-foot cube of it. If the object is being worn or carried by a creature, the creature can make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC to avoid your corroding touch.

If the object touched is either metal armor or a metal shield being worn or carried, its takes a permanent and cumulative -1 penalty to the AC it offers. Armor reduced to an AC of 10 or a shield that drops to a +0 bonus is destroyed. If the object touched is a held metal weapon, it rusts as described in your Rust Body feature.

**Spells (Rusting Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Rust Blast (Tasha's Caustic Brew; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Rust Arrow (Melf's Acid Arrow; 2 charges), Rusting Sphere (Vitriolic Sphere; 4 charges), Transmute Rock to Mud (but only for unworn and unheld metal to rust; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Kingdom of Decay).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to release an aura of intense corrosion in a 30-foot radius centered on yourself. This aura turns the ground into a rust-colored, metal-corroding field. Every unworn and unheld metallic object or creature that starts its turn or enters the area for the first time must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. Constructs made of metal have disadvantage on this saving throw. Unworn and unheld objects corrode instantly, and creatures take 5d10 acid damage on a failed save, or half as much on a successful one. A creature's held or worn metallic objects take a permanent and cumulative -1 penalty, as described in your Rust Body and Corroding Touch features, if it fails the save.  This effect lasts for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.






##### Shiro Shiro no Mi (Castle)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A silver fruit with hard, angular facets similar to castle turrets, crowned by a flag-like stem.

**Description.** The user of this devil fruit transforms into a living fortress, capable of enclosing allies for protection or to strategize, and possesses the ability to generate castle-like structures and weapons.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Fortress Body.** As an action, you can absorb any willing creature or large or smaller object within 5 feet of you into your body. A creature or object absorbed into you becomes tiny while within you and treats your body interior as if it were Mordenkainen's Magnificent Mansion. It gains full cover from within your body and half cover while looking outside the orifices on your body, which are treated as battlements. A ranged weapon used within your body targeting a creature outside it is treated as a regular ranged weapon attack, regardless of the user's size.

**Interior Manipulation.** While in your fortress form, you can reshape the rooms, hallways, mundane objects, furniture, and other structures inside you at will. You can create traps, barriers, or beneficial features like healing rooms, which can heal allies for 2d6+4 hit points once per short rest. You can spend an action to eject a creature from your Fortress Body into an empty space within 10 feet of you.

**Castle Cannons.** Once per turn, while at least one creature is within your fortress body, you can use 1 devil fruit charge as an action to activate castle-mounted cannons that fire at a target you can see within 60 feet. The target must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or take 3d10 bludgeoning damage.

**Spells (Castle Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Castle Tank (Longstrider; Self; 1 charge), Stoneskin (Self; 4 charges), Conjure Volley (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Majestic Bastion).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to enter an enhanced Fortress Body Form to instead become a colossal fortress, as if using the Mighty Fortress spell. You can absorb any allied creature, weapons, or huge or smaller objects within 30 feet into you when you first enter this form. You cannot attack or cast spells while in this form, you can only walk, and your walking speed becomes 40 ft. This form has resistance to all damage except force, and all damage dealt to its walls is also dealt to you. This effect lasts for 10 minutes or until you fall unconscious. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

\page


##### Suke Suke no Mi (Invisibility)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A clear, almost translucent fruit with subtle shimmering patterns that play across its surface.

**Description.** This devil fruit bestows its user the power to become invisible at will. Not only can the user render themselves unseen, but also anything they touch, allowing them to move stealthily or execute surprise attacks.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Vanish from Sight.** As an action, you can become invisible. This effect remains as long as you concentrate (as if concentrating on a spell) up to an hour. Anything you are wearing or carrying becomes invisible with you. Attacking or casting a spell ends the invisibility.

**Cloak Others.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to touch another creature or object to render it invisible for up to 10 minutes. The invisibility ends early if the targeted creature attacks or casts a spell. You can use this ability on one creature or object at a time, using another action to end the effect early. 

**Spells (Invisibility Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: See Invisibility (2 charges), Nondetection (3 charges), Greater Invisibility (4 charges), Mislead (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Realm of Unseen).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to create a 30-foot radius sphere of invisibility centered on yourself. Anything inside this sphere, including other creatures, becomes invisible. The sphere moves with you and lasts for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. Only you and creatures you choose inside the sphere can see other invisible creatures in the sphere but unselected creatures cannot. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

```





##### Supa Supa no Mi (Bladed)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A steely blue-gray fruit, its surface covered in overlapping, blade-like scales, with a stem that looks like a twisted, sharpened spike.

**Description.** This devil fruit empowers its user with the ability to transform any part of their body into sharp blades. The blades are incredibly tough, sharp enough to cut through most materials with ease.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Blade Body.** As a bonus action, you can transform any part of your body into a melee weapon which deals slashing damage. This can range from turning an arm into a longsword, fingers into dagger-like blades, or even combining your arms or legs into a greatsword. Weapons you create have the same properties as their normal counterparts but are considered magical for the purpose of overcoming resistance. You can use this part of your body as a weapon attack, and you are proficient with it. You can only use one weapon active this way at a time, and can dismiss it using a bonus action.

**Steel Skin.** Your AC can’t be less than 18, regardless of what kind of armor you are wearing. By spending 1 devil fruit charge as a bonus action, you can gain a +2 bonus to your AC for up to 1 minute or until you fall unconscious (this effect doesn't stack).

**Cyclone of Slices.** You can create a number of blades from your body and spin to attack with them. You learn the sword burst cantrip. 

**Spells (Bladed Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Thunderous Smite (1 charge), Cloud of Daggers (2 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Staggering Smite (4 charges), Stoneskin (Self; 4 charges), Steel Wind Strike (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Blade Tempest).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Blade Barrier, without expending a spell slot or material components. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

\page


##### Toki Toki no Mi (Future)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A fruit with a golden-hued exterior, looking almost like a radiant, miniature sun with its surface glowing soft light.

**Description.** The bearer of this devil fruit acquires the astonishing capability to send themselves or others forward in time. They cannot, however, rewind time or bring anyone back from the future.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Time Leap.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge and touch a willing creature, sending it forward in time. The target disappears, effectively entering a state of suspended animation, and reappears in the same location up to 20 years into the future in the nearest empty space. If the specified time is not given, the default is 1 day. You can also use this power on yourself.

**Future's Guidance.** As an action, once per 24 hours, you mentally receive an omen for what is to come. This functions similarly to the spell Commune, but comes from a future version of yourself or another creature you temporarily communicate with.

**Spells (Temporal Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Foreshadow (Gift of Alacrity; 1 charge), Future Knowledge (Borrowed Knowledge; 2 charges), Time Shift (Blink; 3 charges), Quicken Time (Haste; 3 charges), Temporal Shunt (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Time's Nexus).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to create a zone where time is in flux within a 30-foot radius centered on yourself. For the next minute or until you fall unconscious, any creature that starts its turn within the zone or enters it for the first time must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failure, the creature is sent 1 round into the future and temporarily disappearing, effectively losing its next turn. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

```




##### Wara Wara no Mi (Straw)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A golden-yellow, grainy-textured pear, tied with a green leafy bow.

**Description.** This devil fruit empowers its user to create, control, and transform into straw at will. The straw crafted by this power isn't ordinary; it has the unique capability to redirect damage dealt to it, turning the tide of battle in unexpected ways.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Straw Doll.** As an action, you can create a small straw voodoo doll of a willing creature you touch. If a creature is unwilling, it must make a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save or if the target is willing, you produce a tiny doll version of that creature which is linked to it, and then absorb it into your body. While you hold at least one doll in your body, any damage you are dealt can instead be redirected to a creature linked to the corresponding doll you contain. If a creature with a linked doll you contain drops to 0 hit points, its corresponding doll is destroyed. Alternatively, you can use a bonus action to expel a doll linked to a creature and negate the effect of this ability on that creature. You can hold up to 10 straw voodoo dolls this way.

**Straw Monster.** As an action, you can spend 4 or more devil fruit charges to use the Summon Construct spell (Clay), which summons a straw monster that fights for you. You can spend additional devil fruit charges to cast it at higher levels (1 charge per total spell level).

**Spells (Straw Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Entangle (1 charge), Spike Growth (2 charges), Straw Form (Guardian of Nature, great tree form only; 4 charges), Compulsion (only targets creatures with straw dolls and save made at disadvantage; 4 charges), Dominate Person (only a target with a straw doll and save made at disadvantage; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Straw Invulnerability).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to enter an invulnerable straw form for 1 minute. You must concentrate to maintain this form as if it were a spell. During this awakening, you appear as a god-like straw being and you redirect all the damage you take, except force damage, onto the environment around you. When you are hit by an attack or damaging effect in this form, a nomagical object of your choice that isn't being held or worn within 60 feet of you takes the damage instead of you. Once used, you can't use this action again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

\page


##### Yomi Yomi no Mi (Resurrection)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enahncer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** An orange citrus fruit vaguely resembling the shape of a skull.

**Description.** This incredible devil fruit grants the user a second chance at life after death, imbuing them with spectral powers sourced from the underworld.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Rebirth.** Upon dying, your soul does not pass on. Instead, after 1 minute, your soul returns to you and you resurrect at the spot of your physical body's death with half of your maximum hit points. This resurrection purges any poisons, diseases, or other conditions afflicting you. This does not work if your physical body is completely destroyed.

**Spectral Form.** As a bonus action, you can assume a ghostly, intangible form for up to 10 minutes. While in this form, you can move through other creatures and objects as if they were difficult terrain, though ending your movement inside an object deals 1d10 force damage to you. Attacks against you have disadvantage, and you have immunity to non-magical damage. Your physical body is temporarily separated from you while you are in this form, and is left incapacitated in the spot where you first used this ability until you return to it instantly by spending a bonus action or waiting until the end of the duration. Your spectral form and physical body share hit points.

In your spectral form, you can't fall and remain hovering in the air even when stunned or otherwise incapacitated. You can't talk or manipulate objects, and any objects you were carrying or holding can't be dropped, used, or otherwise interacted with. You also can't attack or cast spells.

**Gift of the Underworld.** You learn the chill touch cantrip, and your melee weapon attacks deal an extra 1d8 cold damage. Additionally, you can spend an action to re-attach any limbs you are missing. 

**Spells (Underworld Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Ice Slash (Ice Knife; 1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Hunger of Hadar (3 charges), Fear (3 charges), Underworld Barrage (Ice Storm; 4 charges), Soul Parade (Cone of Cold; 5 charges), Greater Restoration (Self; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Underworld Release).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to channel the amazing power of the underworld around you for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. So long as you are conscious, at the start of each of your turns for the duration, all dead creatures of your choice within 30 feet of you are resurrected, as if brought back by the Revivify spell.  Once you activate this awakening, you can't do so again for another 24 hours.

##### Ele Ele No Mi (Electricity)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A bright yellow fruit with a jagged, crackling pattern across its surface.

**Description.** Bestowing the might of the electric element, this devil fruit grants the user the ability to generate, control, and emit electricity. The holder can electrify their surroundings and channel raw energy.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Static Body.** You learn the Shocking Grasp cantrip. Additionally, you are immune to lightning damage.

**Electrical Discharge.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge to emit a wave of electricity in a 15-foot radius around you. Creatures in this area must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, creatures take 3d6 lightning damage, and half as much on a success. The lightning enables or disables (your choice) any electrical device in the area until the end of your next turn.

**Static Field.** As a bonus action, for up to 1 hour or until you fall unconscious, you can raise the electrical current through your body to such an extent that any creature making a melee attack against you and hits within 5 feet takes 1d6 lightning damage. A creature which touches you or starts its turn in contact with you also takes 1d6 lightning damage. You can end this effect early as a bonus action.

**Spells (Electric Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Witch Bolt (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Lightning Bolt (3 charges), Storm Sphere (4 charges), Shocking Current (Immolation; deals lightning damage instead of fire; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Static Blast).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Chain Lightning at the 7th level, without expending a spell slot or material components. Additionally, any electrical devices within 150 feet of you are enabled or disabled (your choice) for 1 minute. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

```


##### Wobba Wobba No Mi (Wobbling)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environemnt Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A jelly-like, translucent fruit with an iridescent sheen, mimicking the look of a wobbling gelatin. It's slightly squishy to the touch and has a spiral, coiling stem.

**Description.** This quirky devil fruit grants the user the ability to induce wobbling vibrations in both living beings and inanimate objects, causing unpredictable disruptions and alterations in their structure and function.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Bounce Back.** When hit by a melee attack, you can use your reaction and spend 5 devil fruit charges to wobble your form, causing the damage to become 0. The attacker must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the attacker takes half of the damage they would have dealt to you, as the force is bounced back to them.

**Wobble Infusion.** As an action, you can touch an object or creature, making it wobble uncontrollably for up to 1 minute. Non-living objects have their functions disrupted (e.g., a locked door might wobble open, a sword might wobble making it harder to wield). Creatures affected must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC at the start of each of their turns. On a failed save, they are considered to have disadvantage on all attack rolls, ability checks, and saving throws until the start of their next turn due to the wobbling. Once a creature saves, it is no longer affected by this ability.

**Wobble Wave.** As an action, you can spend 1 devil fruit charge emit a wave of wobbling energy in a 15-foot cone. All objects and creatures within the area are affected as if by the Wobble Infusion. Creatures in the area must also make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be knocked prone.

**Spells (Wobble Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Earth Tremor (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Erupting Earth (3 cahrges), Confusion (3 charges), Gravity Sinkhole (4 charges), Wrath of Nature (caused by precisely wobbling the earth; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Reality Tremor).** Once you've awakened your power, you can, as an action, induce a fundamental wobble in the very fabric of reality within a 60-foot radius centered on you. For 1 minute or until you fall unconscious, the ground, air, and everything within the area starts to wobble and shift. Every creature except you within the area have disadvantage on attack rolls, ability checks, and saving throws. Additionally, any spells cast within or into the area have a 25% chance to fail, as the wobbling reality distorts their effects. Once you activate this awakening, you can't do so again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 2 | RARE PARAMECIA

##### Gami Gami No Mi (Origami)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** A pale, folded fruit with an ornate polygonal shape. The fruit's stem appears twisted, like a thin strip of folded paper.

**Description.** This unique devil fruit grants the user the artistry of origami on a grand and magical scale, allowing them to fold and manipulate objects and creatures as if they were paper, as well as turn their own body into a paper-like form.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Paper Folding.** As an action, you can touch a creature and force it to make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failure, it is folded in half like paper causing it to become incapacitated for 1 minute. An affected creature can repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success.

**Origami Forms.** As an action, you can touch an allied creature or yourself and transform the target into an origami form for 1 minute, or until you or the creature transform back using a bonus action. You can choose one of the following origami forms which gives its own benefits (doesn't stack):

- **Paper Plane:** When you fall at least 10 feet above the ground, you can use your reaction to extend your paper wings to glide horizontally a number of feet equal to your walking speed, and you take 0 damage from the fall. You determine the direction of the glide.

- **Paper Boat:** You can float and walk on water at a speed equal to your walking speed.

- **Paper Frog:** Your long jump is up to 20 feet and your high jump is up to 10 feet, with or without a running start.

- **Paper Elephant:** You gain a 10 temporary hit points.

- **Paper Fox:** You gain a +10 feet bonus to your walking speed.

**Spells (Origami Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Find Familiar (Origami-Themed Familiar; 1 charge), Paper Fall (Feather Fall; 1 charge), Paper Wings (Fly; Self; 3 charges), Fabricate (folding objects into new shapes; 4 charges), Origami Hand (as Bigby's Hand but made of origami paper; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Origami Vortex).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Whirlwind, without expending a spell slot or material components, as origami birds emerge and create a vortex of wind. Additionally, you and allied creatures within 300 feet of you grow paper wings and gain 60 feet of flying speed for the duration of Whirlwind (and do not take fall damage if they fall immediately after this ability is used). You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.

```



##### Shuffu Shuffu No Mi (Playing Cards)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Substance Generator Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** This fruit is a white apple with playing card suits decorating its surface, and its stem mimics the appearance of a joker card.

**Description.** This enigmatic devil fruit bestows the power of playing cards upon its user. The wielder can manifest and manipulate playing cards with varying effects and even adopt traits from the cards themselves.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Card Manifestation.** As an action, you can produce up to 52 playing cards from your hands. These cards are razor-sharp and can be thrown as ranged weapons with a range of 30/90 feet, dealing 1d6 slashing damage on a hit. You cannot use this action again to produce playing cards until the next dawn. You can only have up to 52 playing cards at a time.

**Card Suit Abilities.** You can infuse your actions with the power of one of the card suits. As a bonus action, you burn a number of cards based on the suit to adopt one of the following stances, which lasts until the start of your next turn:

- **Hearts (12 cards):** When you or an ally within 30 feet are targeted by an attack, you can use your reaction to attempt to block the attack being made against the target with cards. The attack is instead made at disadvantage. You must declare this reaction before the result of the attack roll is given.

- **Diamonds (9 cards):** Any card-based attacks you make deal an additional 2d8 radiant damage as they gleam with a dazzling shine.

- **Clubs (4 cards):** You can use your cards as a melee weapon, dealing 2d8 bludgeoning damage on a hit.

- **Spades (1 card):** You can dig or tunnel through the ground up to 10 feet during you turn with your card, as it slices through solid materials like a shovel through dirt.

**Spells (Card Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Numbered Cards (Magic Missile; 1 charge; can be casted at higher levels by spending additional charges), Face Cards (Crown of Madness; 2 charges), Ace (Fireball; 3 charges), or Joker (Mislead; 5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Final Draw).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to regain all expended playing cards which are reshuffled into your hand and cast Crown of Stars (with glowing cards instead of motes of light). Once you activate this awakening, you can't do so again for another 24 hours.

##### Moa Moa No Mi (Increasing Quality)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** This fruit resembles a gleaming, oversized pearl with shimmering hues of blue and silver. Its surface pulses with a soft light, and has a swirling, thick stem.

**Description.** The Moa Moa No Mi grants its user the incredible ability to amplify the inherent qualities of any object or creature they touch, making them larger, faster, and more potent.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Qualitative Touch.** You learn the Magic Stone cantrip. As an action, you can touch an object or creature. Depending on your intent, you can magnify one of the following qualities:

- **Size:** You can increase the size of the touched object or creature by one category (up to gargantuan). If a creature is enlarged in this manner, it gains the benefits of the Enlarge/Reduce spell (only enlarge). This increase lasts for 1 minute.

- **Speed:** You double the movement speed of the touched object or creature for 1 round.

- **Strength:** You amplify the strength of the touched object or creature. If an object is enhanced, its damage threshold increases by 20. If a creature is enhanced in this manner, it gains advantage on Strength checks, Strength Saves, and Strength-based attack rolls. This boost lasts for 1 round.

**Empowerment Pulse.** As an action, you can expend 1 devil fruit charge to release a wave of energy in a 30-foot radius. All allies within this radius have one of the qualities (Size, Speed, or Strength) enhanced, as per your Qualitative Touch, until the end of your next turn.

**Spells (Amplification Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Catapult (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Jump (1 charge), Enhance Ability (2 charges), Conjure Barrage (3 charges), Haste (3 charges), Freedom of Movement (4 charges), Conjure Volley (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Qualitative Realm).** Once you've awakened your power, as an action you can envelop a 30-foot radius around you in a shimmering dome for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. Within this realm, the very air seems charged with energy. All objects and allies inside gain all the benefits of your Qualitative Touch simultaneously, while enemies find one of their qualities diminished if they fail a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC when the dome is created (Size is reduced by one category, Speed is halved, or Strength-based attacks deal 1d4 less damage) for the duration. A creature which has its equalities diminished can repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns. Once you activate this awakening, you can't do so again for another 24 hours.






##### Buki Buki No Mi (Armory)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** The Buki Buki no Mi looks akin to a steel-gray pomegranate with sharp, angular facets. Its sheen reflects light as if made of polished metal, and the stem is shaped like the handle of a small dagger.

**Description.** The Buki Buki No Mi allows its user to transform parts of their body, or even their entire form, into various weapons. This unique power renders the user a veritable one-person armory, aptly termed a Full-Body Weapon Human.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Weapon Morphing.** As a bonus action, you can transform a part of your body into any weapon (e.g., swords, shields, bows, firearms, etc.), it's considered magical for the purpose of overcoming resistance. You can use this part of your body as a weapon attack, and you are proficient with it. You can only use one weapon active this way at a time, and can dismiss it using a bonus action.

**Full-Body Arsenal.** As an action, you can morph your entire body into a larger weapon or siege equipment (like a ballista or catapult). While in this form, you cannot move or take other actions, but allies can use the weaponized form to attack. This transformation lasts for 1 minute or until you end it as a bonus action.

**Impenetrable Defense.** Your AC can’t be less than 18, regardless of what kind of armor you are wearing. By spending 1 devil fruit charge as a bonus action, you can gain a +2 bonus to your AC for up to 1 minute or until you fall unconscious (this effect doesn't stack).

**Spells (Weapon Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Thunderous Smite (1 charge), Cloud of Daggers (2 charges, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Conjure Barrage (3 charges), Staggering Smite (4 charges), Stoneskin (Self; 4 charges), Conjure Volley (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Living Armory).** Once you've awakened your power, as an action, you create a whirlwind of shifting weaponry around you for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. Blades, firearms, and other armaments constantly morph and reshape across your body. For the next minute, whenever a creature starts its turn within 30 feet of you or moves into that area for the first time on a turn it must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failure, it takes 6d10 bludgeoning, piercing or, slashing damage from the weapons, or half as much on a success. After using this feature, you cannot use it again for another 24 hours.

##### Senko Senko No Mi (Flash)
*Devil Fruit, Rare*

**Type.** Body Enhancer Paramecia

**Fruit appearance.** The Senko Senko no Mi is a radiant, lemon-yellow fruit that appears to softly glow from within, even in complete darkness.

**Description.** The Senko Senko No Mi grants the user the ability to harness and control light, allowing them to create blinding flashes, become a being of pure light, or even manipulate the perceptions of others through illusions.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Light Being.** You are immune to radiant damage and the blinded condition.

Additionally, you emit bright light in a 15-foot radius and dim light for an additional 15 feet. You can turn this light on or off as a bonus action. You can use an action to expand or reduce the radius of bright and dim light by 5 feet each, to a maximum of 30 feet each or a minimum of 10 feet each.

**Blinding Flash.** As an action, you can release a powerful burst of light from your body. All creatures within a 30-foot radius must make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be blinded until the end of their next turn.

**Spells (Flash Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 9 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Faerie Fire (1 charge), Mirror Image (2 charges), Daylight (3 charges), Blinding Smite (3 charges), Sickening Radiance (4 charges), Wall of Light (5 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.

**Awakening (Prismatic Surge).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Sunburst, without expending a spell slot or material components. You can't use this action again for another 24 hours.
