##### Example: Moku Moku no Mi (Smoke)
*Devil Fruit, Very Rare*

**Type.** Gaseous Logia

	
**Fruit appearance.** Puffy and extremely light white melon with cloud-like swirls and a swirly green stem.
	
**Description.** Allows its user to create, control, and transform into smoke at will.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Logia Immunity.** You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through your smoke body. Additionally, you can see normally through smoke, cloud, and fog-like effects that cause an area to become lightly or heavily obscured.
	
**Elemental Form.** You can use the "Logia Elemental Form" feature listed under "Designing a Logia Devil Fruit Sheet".
	
**Smoke Strike.** You learn the mage hand cantrip. Additionally, when you make a melee weapon attack on your turn, you can make its reach extend up to 30 feet by stretching your smoke limbs.

**Smoke Screen.** You can use the Fog Cloud spell at will, casting at the 1st level, without expending a spell slot, charge, or material components. You can cast it at higher levels by spending a Devil Fruit charge for each level you cast it higher.

**Smoke Prison.** As an action during your turn, you can target any number of creaturs within any of your smoke or fog spell areas. Each creature must succeed on a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or become restrained for the duration of the smoke or fog (Escape DC equal to your Devil Fruit save DC).

**Spells (Smoke Plumes).** This devil fruit power has 13 charges. Using your ability to produce smoke, you can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Misty Step (2 charges), Gaseous Form (3 charges), Stinking Cloud (3 charges), Cloudkill (5 charges), Investiture of Wind (6 charges), Wind Walk (6 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Explosive Plume).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Incendiary Cloud without expending any charges or material components. You can’t use this feature again for another 24 hours.




  





CHAPTER 3 | VERY RARE LOGIA

\page


##### Yuki Yuki no Mi (Snow)
*Devil Fruit, Very Rare*

**Type.** Solid Logia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A white and light blue starfruit with snowflake patterns.
	
**Description.** Allows its user to create, control, and transform into snow at will.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Logia Immunity.** You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through your snow body. Additionally, you are immune to cold damage and you can move across Difficult Terrain created by ice or snow without spending extra Movement.

**Elemental Form.** You can use the "Logia Elemental Form" feature listed under "Designing a Logia Devil Fruit Sheet".
	
**Crippling Frost.** You learn the Frostbite Cantrip. Any time a creature takes cold damage from your Devil Fruit Spells or Cantrip, its speed is reduced by 10 until the start of your next turn.

**Snow Demon.** As an action, you can spend 3 devil fruit charges to enter a snow demon form for 1 minute. When you do so, your size grows to large, you gain 30 temporary hit points, and you grow an icy fanged maw, which is a natural weapon you can use to make unarmed strikes for the duration. If you hit with it, you deal piercing damage equal to 2d6, plus an additional 1d6 cold damage, instead of the bludgeoning damage normal for an unarmed strike. Additionally, when you hit a creature with your bite attack in this form, it must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or become stunned until the start of your next turn.
	
**Spells (Snow Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 13 charges. You can use an action, bonus action, or reaction and expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: armor of agathys (1 charge, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), snilloc's snowball swarm (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), elemental weapon (cold; 3 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), ice storm (4 charges), cone of cold (5 charges), investiture of ice (6 charges), wall of ice (6 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Ten-Layer Igloo).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Prismatic Wall, with each layer being Blue, without expending any charges or material components. You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.



```
```



##### Numa Numa no Mi (Swamp)
*Devil Fruit, Very Rare*

**Type.** Liquid Logia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A light brown pear with drooping s-shaped swirl patterns, which smells of sulfur.
	
**Description.** Allows its user to create, control, and transform into mud and other liquid "swamp" elements at will.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Logia Immunity.** You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through your swamp body. Additionally, you can move across Difficult Terrain created by mud or swamps without spending extra Movement, and you do not suffocate inside of your swamp waters.

**Elemental Form.** You can use the "Logia Elemental Form" feature listed under "Designing a Logia Devil Fruit Sheet".
	
**Swampy Storage.** You learn the Mold Earth Cantrip. Additionally, you can store additional equipment inside your swamp body, multiplying your carrying capacity by 10.

**Swamp Trap.** As an action, you can transform a 5-foot diameter section of dirt or rock you can see within 30 feet of you into a swampy sinkhole, which is 20 feet deep. This sinking ground remains this way for 10 minutes or until you return it back to normal as a bonus action. This area is considered difficult terrain when walked across, and a creature which moves into it or starts its turn standing in the area must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failure, the creature is restrained and sinks 5 feet deeper into the hole at the start of each of its turn. A creature can repeat the Strength saving throw at the start of each of its turns to escape, after which it then must use at least 20 feet of movement to crawl out of the swampy hole. A creature which is fully submerged in the swampy hole begins to suffocate and is blinded and deafened for the duration, but it doesn't trigger a Devil Fruit user's Sea Weakness.
	
**Spells (Swamp Control).** This devil fruit power has 13 charges. You can use an action, bonus action, or reaction and expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: earth tremor (1 charge, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), entangle (1 charge), maximillian's earthen grasp (2 charges), wall of water (made of muddy swamp material; 3 charges), stone shape (4 charges), transmute rock (5 charges), move earth (6 charges), investiture of stone (6 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Calamity Swamp).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cause all ground within 120 feet of you to become affected by your Swamp Trap feature for 10 minutes. Additionally, your allies can move through the terrain normally without sinking or needing to spend extra movement. You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 3 | VERY RARE LOGIA

\page


##### Gasu Gasu no Mi (Gas)
*Devil Fruit, Very Rare*

**Type.** Gaseous Logia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A small neon light purple melon with cloud-like swirl patterns.
	
**Description.** Allows its user to create, control, and transform into various gases at will.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Logia Immunity.** You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through your gas body. You are immune to poison damage and the poisoned condition, and you are immune to suffocating, but not from drowning.

**Elemental Form.** You can use the "Logia Elemental Form" feature listed under "Designing a Logia Devil Fruit Sheet".
	
**Gas Control.** You learn the Gust, Thaumaturgy, and Produce flame Cantrips, no material components required. Additionally, you can use a bonus action to create or remove oxygen up to 30 feet around you for up to 10 minutes (see suffocating rules in the D&D Dungeon Master’s Guide).
	
**Spells (Deadly Gases).** This devil fruit power has 13 charges. You can use an action, bonus action, or reaction and expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: chromatic orb (1 charge, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), sleep (1 charge, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), flame blade (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), gust of wind (2 charges), warding wind (2 charges), gaseous form (3 charges), stinking cloud (3 charges), wind wall (3 charges), fireball (3 charges), cloudkill (5 charges), Investiture of Wind (6 charges), prismatic spray (7 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Terror Gas).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Weird, without expending any charges or material components. You can’t use this action for another 24 hours.



```
```


##### Suna Suna no Mi (Sand)
*Devil Fruit, Very Rare*

**Type.** Gaseous Logia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A tan cactus shaped like a ball with swirling patterns.
	
**Description.** Allows its user to create, control, and transform into sand at will.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Logia Immunity.** You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through your sand body. Additionally, you can move across Difficult Terrain created by desserts without spending extra Movement.

**Elemental Form.** You can use the "Logia Elemental Form" feature listed under "Designing a Logia Devil Fruit Sheet".
	
**Dry Sands.** You learn the Mold Earth and Toll the Dead Cantrips. Additionally, any creature that fails its save against one of your Devil Fruit spells or abilities which deal necrotic damage becomes dehydrated until the start of your next turn. A dehydrated creature gains two temporary levels of exhaustion until the start of your next turn.

**Dessert Sword.** As an action, you can spend 3 devil fruit charges to create a large piercing sand blade. When you do so, you can fire a beam of sand, forming a line of 100 feet long and 5 feet wide out from you in a direction you choose. Each creature in the line must make a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. A creature takes 3d6 piercing damage and 3d6 necrotic damage on a failed save. and is dehydrated until the start of your next turn, or half as much damage on a successful one and isn't dehydrated. You can spend additional devil fruit charges to increase the piercing damage by 1d6 for each additional charge spent, up to a total of 9d6 piercing damage and 3d6 necrotic damage.
	
**Spells (Desert Sands).** This devil fruit power has 13 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: earth tremor (1 charge, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), dust devil (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), gaseous form (3 charges), wall of sand (3 charges), blight (4 charges), transmute rock (5 charges), investiture of wind (6 charges), circle of death (6 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Ground Death).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Abi-Dalzim's Horrid Wilting, without expending any charges or material components. You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 3 | VERY RARE LOGIA

\page

# Legendary Devil Fruits


##### Ope Ope no Mi (Surgery) Part 1
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A red heart-shaped melon with swirls
	
**Description.** Allows the user to create a zone of control around them that they can manipulate in a variety of ways.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Counter Shock & Room.** You learn the Shocking Grasp cantrip. Additionally, you can use a bonus action to create a 60-foot radius psychic sphere, or "room", centered on where you are standing when you create it. You must maintain concentration on this room (as if concentrating on a spell). The room lasts for 1 minute, or until you end it using a bonus action. You can only have one room up at a time. Each turn, you can use an another bonus action to increase the radius of the room by another 60 feet. Any creature you can see within the room can be targeted by any leveled spell casted using this devil fruit under "Room Spells", regardless of spell range. Additionally, the range of spells or any spell effect listed in "room spells" can be extended to anywhere within the "room", but is also limited by the range of the room and cannot be cast outside it or affect anything outside the room's radius. For example, misty step's range increases from 60 feet up to the range of anywhere within the room's radius. Room Spells which normally require concentration don't require concentration while cast within the Room's radius, but will end when the Room's duration ends or when you lose concentration on the room.

You can spend an action to Scan the radius of your room to spot a creature you are aware of that is behind full cover or hidden within the room's range. You can do this by rolling a perception check against the creature's stealth to locate it. A creature spotted this way cannot gain the benefits of full cover against your Devil Fruit Spells while within the room's range, and can be seen by you as if they were fully visible, becoming outlined by Faerie Fire.

**Surgery Scalpel.** As an action, you can designate a melee weapon you are proficient with that deals slashing or piercing damage as your Surgery Scalpel when using your Ope Ope no Mi powers. The weapon becomes magical for the purpose of overcoming resistance if it isn't already. Additionally, when you hit a creature within your Room with your Surgery Scalpel, once per turn you can forego dealing damage and instead use one of the following effects against the target:

- **Injection Shot:** You can spend 1 devil fruit charge to deal an extra 2d8 necrotic damage to the target with your Surgery Scalpel.

- **Gamma Knife:** You can spend 3 devil fruit charges to deal an extra 3d8 radiant damage to the target with your Surgery Scalpel. Additionally, the creature must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or become poisoned for 1 minute. The target can repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turn, ending the condition on a success.

- **Amputate:** You cleanly slice off one of the creature's limbs for 10 minutes, but dealing no harm to it in the process. Each time you remove a creature's limbs this way, it gains a level of exhaustion (up to a maximum of 5 levels of exhaustion) so long as the limbs aren't attached. A creature that has had its limbs removed this way can spend an action to re-attach all its limbs, ending all levels of exhaustion applied by the amputation on itself. You can spend 1 devil fruit charge when using this attack during your turn to apply "Radio Knife" to the Amputation, dealing 1d8 electric damage to the target, and causing the creature to become unable to re-attach it's missing limb unless its succeeds on a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC as a part of its action to re-attach its limbs. If the creature fails the saving throw, its action is wasted and its limbs remain unattached.


**Shambles.** You can target two creatures or objects, including yourself, within your "room" as an action. The two targets magically teleport to each other's spaces and swap places.

**Immortality Surgery.** By spending 10 minutes operating on another creature, you grant it immortality. The target stops aging. It is immune to any effect that would age it, and it can't die from old age. However, you will die and be reduced to dust upon completing this surgery.
	
**Room Spells.** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. While within the "room", you can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: catapult (1 charge, can be cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), detect poison and disease (1 charge), cure wounds (1 charge, can be cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), find traps (2 charges), hold person (2 charges, can be cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), levitate (2 charges), silence (2 charges), see invisibility (only within room; 2 charges), vortex warp (2 charges), gravity sinkhole (4 charges), hold monster (5 charges), mass cure wounds (5 charges), telekinesis (5 charges), move earth (6 charges), whirlwind (7 charges), or tether essence (7 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.





CHAPTER 4 | LEGENDARY PARAMECIA

\page


##### Ope Ope no Mi (Surgery) Part 2
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Awakening (K-ROOM and R-ROOM).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to activate K-ROOM or R-ROOM, or use an action to alternate between the two, ending any currently active Rooms. You can use either of these special rooms for 1 minute after activating your awakening (but cannot activate your regular Room or both at the same time), or until you fall unconscious, and they do not require concentration to maintain:

- **K-ROOM:** You apply your Room to your designated Surgery Scalpel as a special coating for the duration. While this special Room is active, your Surgery Scalpel weapon's reach becomes 60 feet. You can use a bonus action while your K-ROOM coating is active to extend your Surgery Scalpel's reach by an additional 60 feet. Additionally, when you hit a creature with K-ROOM coated Surgery Scalpel, once per turn you can forego dealing damage and instead use one of the following effects against the target:
 - **Shock Surge:** You send a deadly shock through the target, dealing 10d10 lightning damage to it.
 - **Puncture Surge:** The target is pushed away from you to the end of your weapon's reach and knocked prone. If a thrown target strikes a solid surface, the target takes 3 (1d6) bludgeoning damage for every 10 feet it was pushed. If the target is pushed into another creature, that creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or take the same damage and be knocked prone.
 
- **R-ROOM:** You apply your Room to a target within 120 feet of you. The room is a 10-foot-radius sphere which surrounds the target. Until the duration ends, the sphere moves with the target, centered on it. This room acts as an Antimagic Field spell.

You can’t use this feature again for another 24 hours.



```
```


##### Gura Gura no Mi (Earthquake)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A massive light blue pear with S-shaped spiral patterns, which rumbles and shakes occasionally on its own.
	
**Description.** Allows the user to produce catastrophic earthquakes and move the earth and sea with ease.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Quake Immunity.** You are immune to thunder damage.
	
**Mini Quakes.** You learn the Thunderclap and Mold Earth cantrips, no material components required. Additionally, you can cast earth tremor (1st level) as an action, no charges required. You can cast it at higher levels by spending a devil fruit charge for each additional level the spell is cast at.

**Quake Strike.** Once per turn, when you hit with a melee weapon attack, you can expend 1 or more devil fruit charges to release a quake strike. If you do so, the target and all other creatures within 15 feet of you must also make a Constitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failure, a target takes 1d8 thunder damage, plus 1d8 for each charge expended, and is pushed 10 feet away from you. On a success, a target takes half as much thunder damage, and isn't pushed. In addition, unsecured objects that are completely within the area of effect are automatically pushed 10 feet away from you by the attack's effect, and the effect emits a thunderous boom audible out to 300 feet.
	
**Spells (Deadly Quakes).** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: shatter (2 charges, can be cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), thunder step (3 charges), erupting earth (3 charges), move earth (6 charges), gravity fissure (6 charges), investiture of stone (6 charges), tsunami (8 charges), earthquake (8 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Island Shaking).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Island Shaking^ (view Chapter 8 in the Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB), without expending any charges or material components. You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 4 | LEGENDARY PARAMECIA

\page


##### Uta Uta no Mi (Song)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia
	
**Fruit appearance.** a round, pink fruit with multiple colored stripes across it middle section resembling a musical staff, and a green stem shaped like an accented eighth note. 
	
**Description.** Allows the user to bring the consciousness of creature's into a dream world of song by singing.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.
	
**Song World.** As an action, you can sing to all humanoid creatures of your choice that can hear you within 120 feet to attempt to pull them into a special Song World. Each targeted creature must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or magically fall unconscious. A willing creature automatically fails this saving throw. While a creature is unconscious this way, it has its astral body projected into a closed-off section of the Astral Plane (following the rules of the Astral Projection spell), named the "Song World". The Song World closely resembles the real world, and you can manipulate and affect the world and objects or creatures within it using your Devil Fruit powers.

You are able to enter the Song World while you are still conscious, projecting your astral body into the Song World at will. You can control your astral body and physical body at the same time. You can only use your Song World Spells against creatures within your Song World using your astral body and your Song World Spells with a range of Self can only be used on your astral body, not your physical body. Additionally, if you fall unconscious while creatures are within your Song World, their astral bodies are returned to their physical bodies and their physical body regains consciousness.

**Song Puppets.** As an action, if a humanoid creature is unconscious due to your Song World feature, you are able to make its physical body a Song Puppet while it remains unconscious. A Song Puppet is controlled by you as if using the Dominate Person spell, no concentration required.

**Song Minions.** You can use the Animate Objects, Telekinesis, and Mirage Arcane spells at will, without expending a spell slot, charge, or material components. You can cast these spells this way from within the Song World using your astral body.
	
**Song World Spells.** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: shield (1 charge), hold person (2 charges, can be cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), fly (3 charges), dispel magic (3 charges), mass healing word (3 charges), wrath of nature (5 charges), guards and wards (6 charges), project image (7 charges), antimagic field (8 charges), reality break (8 charges), or wish (9 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn. You can only use these spells against a creature's astral body within the song world.
	
**Awakening (Tot Musica).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to summon Tot Musica, the Demon King of Songs, in an empty space within 120 feet of you, for 1 minute, until you fall unconscious or end it as a bonus action. Tot Musica has the stats of an Elder Tempest from Mordenkainen's Tome of Foes. While Tot Musica is alive, the Song World and material plane are temporarily fused for the duration. For the duration, all creatures which have their astral bodies trapped in the Song World have them returned to their physical bodies and regain consciousness, after which their astral bodies are returned back to the Song World as per your Song World ability. Your astral body is also temporarily returned to your physical body for the duration of your awakening. You can use all of your Devil Fruit abilities and Song World Spells within the real world and material plane, casting them from your physical body while the worlds remain fused. Once used, you can’t activate your awakening again for another 24 hours.





CHAPTER 4 | LEGENDARY PARAMECIA

\page


##### Soru Soru no Mi (Soul Manipulation)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia
	
**Fruit appearance.** a large, pink plum with spiral shapes along its surface.
	
**Description.** Allows the user to interact with and manipulate the souls of other living creatures.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.
	
**Soul Pocus.** As an action, you can target a creature that can see and hear you within 60 feet and rip away a part of it's soul to attempt to rob it of it's lifespan. The creature must have a challenge rating of 1/8 or higher for this ability to work on it. The creature must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or the creature takes 10 (3d6) necrotic damage and its hit point maximum is reduced by an amount equal to the damage taken. A creature that is frightened of you has disadvantage on this saving throw. If a creature is immune to the frightened condition or necrotic damage, it is not affected by this ability. This reduction is permanent, unless a Greater Restoration, Heal, or Wish spell is used on the target. The target dies if this effect reduces its hit point maximum to 0. Additionally, whenever a creature fails this saving throw and has its hit point maximum reduced by this ability, you gain 1 devil fruit charge.

Additionally, you can spend an action to sacrifice 10 hit points and reduce your hit point maxmimum by 10 to gain 1 devil fruit charge. This reduction lasts until you complete a long rest.

**Soul Homies.** As an action, you can spend 5 devil fruit charges to create a "Homie" by filling a target with collected soul power. You use the Aniamte Objects or Awaken spell descriptions on applicable targets for this ability. Homies created this way follow your commands and last indefinitely.

Alternatively, you can use this action and spend 9 devil fruit charges to create a Special Homie made of stronger soul energy and raw elemental power. For a special homie, use the Conjure Elemental spell description instead, and you can summon an elemental with a challenge rating of 9 or lower which follows your orders and lasts indefinitely.

**Incarnations.** You can expend 2 devil fruit charges to create an Incarnation within 30 feet of you. An Incarnation has the statistics of a Specter (view the standard 5e monster manual). An Incarnation cannot attack, but can use your Soul Pocus on willing creatures to collect soul energy, though it cannot reduce a creature's maximum hit points below 1. If a creature only has 1 maximum hit point, an Incarnation cannot use Soul Pocus on it. An Incarnation follows your orders and lasts until you dismiss it as a bonus action. It can collect up to 5 devil fruit charges from creatures this way, which it can then transfer to you as an action while it is within 5 feet of you.

**Spells (Soul Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 17 maximum charges, but you start with none. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: chromatic orb (1 charge, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), phantasmal force (2 charges; can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), elemental weapon (3 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), fear (3 charges), fireball (3 charges), lightning bolt (3 charges), Blight (4 charges), Dominate Person (5 charges), Flame Strike (5 charges), Wrath of Nature (5 charges), Chain Lightning (6 charges), Soul Cage (6 charges), Prismatic Spray (7 charges), Fire Storm (7 charges), Feeblemind (8 charges), or Psychic Scream (9 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges when you use your Soul Pocus ability.
	
**Awakening (3000 Leagues of Misery).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to attempt to siphon the souls of all creatures within 60 feet of you. Each creature of your choice in the area is subjected to your Soul Pocus ability and must save against it. Additionally, as a part of this action, you also summon a Soul Monster in an empty space you can see within 60 feet of you, which lasts for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. This Soul monster has the statistics of a Boneclaw from Mordenkainen's Tome of Foes, loses its Reujuvenation feature and gains the Incorporeal Movement feature instead.

The Soul Monster is an ally to you and your companions. In combat, it shares your initiative count, but it takes its turn immediately after yours. It obeys your verbal commands (no action required by you). If you don’t issue any, it takes the Dodge action and uses its move to avoid danger.

Once used, you can’t activate your awakening again for another 24 hours.



CHAPTER 4 | LEGENDARY PARAMECIA

\page


##### Zushi Zushi no Mi (Gravity)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia
	
**Fruit appearance.** An unusually heavy dark gray melon with purple cracks and ripples along its surface.
	
**Description.** Allows the user to create and manipulate gravitational forces.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.
	
**Gravity Control.** You learn the Sapping Sting cantrip, no material components required. Additionally, you can cast magnify gravity (1st level) as an action, no charges required. You can cast it at higher levels by spending a devil fruit charge for each additional level the spell is cast at.

**Gravity Wave.** As an action, you can spend 3 devil fruit charges to emit a large wave of enhanced gravity. When you do so, you can fire a wave of gravitational energy forming a line of 100 feet long and 5 feet wide out from you in a direction you choose. Each creature in the line must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. A creature takes 6d6 force damage on a failed save and is knocked prone, or half as much damage on a successful one and isn't knocked prone. You can spend additional devil fruit charges to increase the force damage by 1d6, up to a total of 12d6 force damage.

**Spells (Gravity Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: immovable object (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), levitate (2 charges), pulse wave (3 charges), gravity sinkhole (4 charges), telekinesis (5 charges), gravity fissure (6 charges), reverse gravity (7 charges), dark star (8 charges), or meteor swarm (9 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Extreme Gravity Field).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to create a 60-foot radius gravity aura around you for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. When you activate this aura, you can designate any number of creatures you can see to be unaffected by it. An affected creature's speed is halved in the area, and when the creature enters the area for the first time on a turn or starts its turn there, it must make a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. On a failed save, the creature takes 10d8 force damage and is knocked prone. On a successful save, the creature takes half as much damage and isn't knocked prone. While in the aura, any object that isn't being worn or carried in the sphere requires a successful Strength check against your spell save DC to pick up or move. Ranged attacks made against you and any creature within this field are made at disadvantage. Once used, you can’t activate your awakening again for another 24 hours.




```
```


##### Fuwa Fuwa no Mi (Floating)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A long yellow pear with black spirals across its surface and a swirling brown stem. It seems to remain stationary, floating in the air even when dropped.
	
**Description.** Allows the user to levitate themselves and non-living things into the air, which can be controlled telepathically.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Permanent Levitation.** As an action, you can touch any object that isn't being worn or held, or up to a 20-foot cube of terrain, and cause it to levitate up to 20 feet in the air (as if using the levitate spell) at will, no concentration required, and regardless of its weight. You can move one object you are levitating up to 20 feet during your turn. You can cause multiple objects to permanently levitate this way, and can end this levitation effect on any number of them as a bonus action. If you fall unconscious, every object you are levitating this way loses its levitating properties and begins to fall if it is midair, unless you command them to levitate again as an action.

**Bodily Levitation.** You gain a flying speed equal to your walking speed, and hover mid-air.

**Spells (Floating Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: catapult (1 charge, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), immovable object (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), control water (4 charges), animate objects (5 charges), move earth (6 charges), reverse gravity (7 charges), earthquake (8 charges), or tsunami (8 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn. These spells only work on objects or regions of terrain you have touched before.
	
**Awakening (Float Zone).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to create a 120-foot radius sphere centered on a point you can see within 300 feet for 1 minute or until you fall unconscious. Any creature or object within this sphere can be targeted by any of your Devil Fruit spells for the duration, even if you haven't touched them before. Additionally, if a creature starts its turn in the sphere or enters it for the first time during its turn, it must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failure, a creature is levitated 20 feet in the air (as if affected by the Levitate spell), and has its movement halved for the rest of its turn. Once used, you can’t activate your awakening again for another 24 hours.





CHAPTER 4 | LEGENDARY PARAMECIA

\page


##### Shima Shima no Mi (Island Control)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Environment Alterer Paramecia
	
**Fruit appearance.** An flat blue melon with siwlrs across it and a green, leafy top. The stem resembles a tree, emerging from the top.
	
**Description.** Allows the user to merge with an island's environment and manipulate it.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.
	
**Stone Meld.** As an action, you can merge with any stone surface, allowing you to traverse through it, effectively disappearing from sight. While merged, you can move within and emerge from any connected stone surface within 60 feet.

**Island Manipulation.** You can use the Stone Shape, Passwall, Transmute Rock, and Wall of Stone spells at will so long as you are touching the ground, without expending a spell slot, charge, or material components. 

**Island Body.** You can spend 4 devil fruit charges to mold the stone around you to polymorph (as if using the polymorph spell) yourself into a stone construct or earth elemental that has a challenge rating equal to or less than your level for up to 1 hour. However, your mental ability scores remain the same and you can speak while in this form. You remain this way as long as you concentrate on maintaining it (as if concentrating on a spell). The transformation lasts for the duration, or until you drop to 0 hit points or die. You can continue to use your Devil Fruit abilities and spells in this form, so long as they don't require concentration, but cannot use any other class or racial features or spells for the duration.

**Spells (Island Techniques).** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Earth Tremor (1 charge, and can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), Maximilian’s Earthen Grasp (2 charges), Erupting Earth (3 charges), Stoneskin (4 charges), Wrath of Nature (5 charges), Investiture of Stone (6 charges), Move Earth (6 charges), Earthquake (8 charges), or Tsunami (8 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Total Island Dominion).** Once you've awakened your power, you can spend an action to polymorph into a Zaratan from Mordenkainen's Tome of Foes for 1 minute, using your Island Body feature. However, you still have a swim speed of 0 in this form and are subject to your Sea Weakness. Once used, you can’t activate your awakening again for another 24 hours.





CHAPTER 4 | LEGENDARY PARAMECIA

\page


##### Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Mythical Zoan

**Fruit appearance.** This devil fruit appears as a bright blue pineapple with swirling flame patterns across its surface, and a bright golden crown.

**Description.** This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a phoenix.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Beast Shape.** As an action, you are able to transform into a *Phoenix* from Mordenkainen's Tome of Foes. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Hybrid Form.** You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Awakening.** Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.



##### Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model: Red Dragon
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Mythical Zoan

**Fruit appearance.** This devil fruit appears as a large, red pear with bright scales across its surface and a flame-shaped leaf emerging from its stem.

**Description.** This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a red dragon.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Beast Shape.** As an action, you are able to transform into an *Adult Red Dragon* from the standard D&D 5th Edition Monster Manual. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Hybrid Form.** You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Awakening.** Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

##### Uma Uma no Mi, Model: Unicorn
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Mythical Zoan

**Fruit appearance.** This devil fruit appears as a shiny pearlescent melon with cloud-like swirls, a rainbow-striped center, and a swirling conical white stem pointing upward.

**Description.** This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a unicorn.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Beast Shape.** As an action, you are able to transform into a *Unicorn* using the stat block to the right. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Hybrid Form.** You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Awakening.** Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

> ## Unicorn
>*Large Celestial, lawful good*
> ___
> - **Armor Class** 16 (natural armor)
> - **Hit Points** 135 (18d10 + 36)
> - **Speed** 50 ft.
>___
>|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
>|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
>|20 (+5)|14 (+2)|15 (+2)|11 (+0)|17 (+3)|16 (+3)|
>___
> - **Damage Immunities** poison
> - **Condition Immunities** charmed, paralyzed, poisoned
> - **Senses** darkvision 60 ft., passive Perception 13
> - **Challenge** 10 (5,900 XP)
> ___
> ***Charge.***  If the unicorn moves at least 20 ft. straight toward a target and then hits it with a horn attack on the same turn, the target takes an extra 9 (2d8) piercing damage. If the target is a creature, it must succeed on a DC 16 Strength saving throw or be knocked prone.
>
> ***Innate Spellcasting.***  The unicorn's innate spellcasting ability is Charisma (spell save DC 14). The unicorn can innately cast the following spells, requiring no components: • At will: detect evil and good, druidcraft, pass without trace • 1/day each: calm emotions, dispel evil and good, entangle
>
> ***Magic Resistance.*** The unicorn has advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.
>
> ***Magic Weapons.*** The unicorn's weapon attacks are magical.
>
> ### Actions
> ***Multiattack.*** The unicorn makes three attacks: two with its hooves and one with its horn.
>
> ***Hooves.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +9 to hit, reach 5ft., one target. *Hit* (2d10 + 5) bludgeoning damage.
>
> ***Horn.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +9 to hit, reach 5ft., one target. *Hit* (2d8 + 5) piercing damage.
>
> ***Healing Touch (3/Day).*** The unicorn touches another creature with its horn. The target magically regains 11 (2d8 + 2) hit points. In addition, the touch removes all diseases and neutralizes all poisons afflicting the target.
>
> ***Teleport (1/Day).*** The unicorn magically teleports itself and up to three willing creatures it can see within 5 ft. of it, along with any equipment they are wearing or carrying, to a location the unicorn is familiar with, up to 1 mile away.


CHAPTER 4 | LEGENDARY ZOAN

\page


##### Inu Inu no Mi, Model: Okuchi no Makami
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Mythical Zoan

**Fruit appearance.** This devil fruit appears as flat orange with swirl patterns emerging from its stem and five leaves connecting to its swirling yellow stem.

**Description.** This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a Okuchi no Makami, aka a Large-Mouthed True/Pure God Dog.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Beast Shape.** As an action, you are able to transform into an *Okuchi no Makami* using the stat block to the right. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Hybrid Form.** You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Awakening.** Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.



___
> ## Okuchi no Makami
>*Huge Celestial, lawful good*
> ___
> - **Armor Class** 16 (natural armor)
> - **Hit Points** 200 (16d12 + 96)
> - **Speed** 50 ft.
>___
>|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
>|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
>|22 (+6)|10 (+0)|22 (+6)| 19 (+4)| 20 (+5)|20 (+5)|
>___
> - **Skills** Perception +9, Insight +9, Religion +9
> - **Damage Immunities** cold
> - **Condition Immunities** charmed, paralyzed, poisoned
> - **Senses** passive Perception 15
> - **Challenge** 13 (10,000 XP)
> ___
> ***Ice Walk.*** The Okuchi no Makami can move across and climb icy surfaces without needing to make an ability check. Additionally, difficult terrain composed of ice or snow doesn't cost it extra moment.
>
> ***Pack Tactics.*** The Okuchi no Makami has advantage on an attack roll against a creature if at least one of the Okuchi no Makami's allies is within 5 ft. of the creature and the ally isn't incapacitated.
>
> ***Snow Camouflage.*** The Okuchi no Makami has advantage on Dexterity (Stealth) checks made to hide in snowy terrain.
>
> ### Actions
> ***Multiattack.*** The Okuchi no Makami makes three attacks: one with its bite and two with its claws.
>
> ***Bite.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +11 to hit, reach 5ft., one target. *Hit* (2d10 + 6) piercing damage plus (1d8) cold damage.
>
> ***Claw.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +11 to hit, reach 5ft., one target. *Hit* (2d6 + 6) slashing damage.
>
> ***Cold Breath (Recharge 5-6).*** The Okuchi no Makami exhales an icy blast in a 60-foot cone. Each creature in that area must make a DC 19 Constitution saving throw, taking 54 (12d8) cold damage on a failed save, or half as much damage on a successful one.

##### Hito Hito no Mi, Model: Planetar
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Mythical Zoan

**Fruit appearance.** This devil fruit appears as a white melon with cloud-like swirls across its surface and a bright golden stem forming a halo above it.

**Description.** This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into a planetar.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Beast Shape.** As an action, you are able to transform into a *Planetar* from the standard D&D 5th Edition Monster Manual. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Hybrid Form.** You can use your action to enter a "hybrid" zoan state, combining a mix of qualities from both your humanoid form and beast form together for a temporary period of time. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

**Awakening.** Upon the awakening of your Zoan Devil Fruit power, when you enter your Hybrid Form, you can temporarily enter your Awakened State, which lasts for 1 minute.

While your Awakened State is active, your hit point maximum and hit points increase by 50, your weapon attacks and unarmed strike attacks deal extra damage of their primary damage type equal to your character level, and you are able to select an additional hybrid form option. Furthermore, at the start of each of your turns for the duration of this state, you regain hit points equivalent to your character level + your Constitution modifier.

Should the duration of your Awakened State expire, you hold the option to extend its span for an additional minute, at the cost of incurring a level of exhaustion. If needed, you can further extend this state by enduring an extra level of exhaustion for each additional minute. These levels of exhaustion can only be removed by completing a long rest.

Once your Awakened State ends, it can't be activated again for another 24 hours.

##### Hito Hito no Mi, Model: Nika
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Mythical Zoan

**Fruit appearance.** This devil fruit appears as spherical violet fruit with S-shaped swirls and bumps across its surface and a horizontal t-shaped flat green stem with a swirl at the right end.

**Description.** This zoan devil fruit allows its user to transform into the sun god Nika.

**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Beast Shape.** As an action, you are able to transform into *Nika* using the stat block to the right. You follow the rules given in Chapter 7 under "Designing a Zoan Devil Fruit Sheet" in the One Piece Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB.

> ## Nika
>*Large Celestial, chaotic good*
> ___
> - **Armor Class** 19 (natural armor)
> - **Hit Points** 300 (24d10 + 168)
> - **Speed** 30 ft., fly 60 ft.
>___
>|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
>|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
>|26 (+8)|20 (+5)|24 (+7)| 19 (+4)| 22 (+6)|25 (+7)|
>___
> - **Saving Throws: Dex +11, Wis +10, Cha +12
> - **Damage Immunities** bludgeoning from nonmagical attacks
> - **Condition Immunities** charmed, frightened
> - **Senses** passive Perception 16
> - **Languages:** Common
> - **Challenge** 20 (25,000 XP)
> ___
> ***Drums of Liberation.*** Any creature friendly to Nika within 30 feet of Nika cannot be frightened while Nika is conscious.
>
> ***Magic Weapons.*** Nika's weapon attacks are magical.
>
> ***Stretchy Limbs.*** Nika's melee weapon attacks have a reach of 30 feet.
>
> ***Innate spellcasting.*** Nika's spellcasting ability is Charisma (spell save DC 21). Nika can innately cast the following spells, requiring no material components:
>
>• At will: arms of hadar, earth tremor, enlarge/reduce (Self)
>
>• 3/day each:  call lightning, erupting earth, freedom of movement (Self)
>
>• 1/day each: bigby's hand (opaque hand which replaces one of Nika's fists), move earth, wall of stone
>
> ### Actions
> ***Multiattack.*** Nika makes four unarmed strikes.
>
> ***Unarmed Strike.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +14 to hit, reach 30ft., one target. *Hit* (6d8 + 8) piercing damage, plus 9 (2d8) bludgeoning damage. The target takes the secondary bludgeoning damage if Nika is using its Colossal Growth.
>
> ***Colossal Growth (1/day).*** Nika polymorphs into a giant, with its size increasing to gargantuan, for 1 minute. Nika's stats remain the same in this form, and its Unarmed Strikes deal an extra 2d8 bludgeoning damage while polymorphed. It reverts to its true form if it falls to 0 hit points or falls unconscious.

##### Pika Pika no Mi (Light)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Gaseous Logia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A bright yellow starfruit with sharp swirling patterns and several sharp protrusions on its surface.
	
**Description.** Allows its user to create, control, and transform into light at will.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Logia Immunity.** You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through your light body. Additionally, you are immune to radiant damage and the blinded condition.

**Elemental Form.** You can use the "Logia Elemental Form" feature listed under "Designing a Logia Devil Fruit Sheet".
	
**Radiant Body.** You learn the Word of Radiance, Light, and Dancing Lights Cantrips, no material components required. Additionally, you can cast guiding bolt (1st level) as an action, no charges required. You can cast it at higher levels by spending a devil fruit charge for each additional level the spell is cast at.

**Sacred Mirror.** You can expend 1 devil fruit charge as an action to direct your light form at blinding speeds in order to teleport, along with any equipment you are wearing or carrying, up to 120 feet to an unoccupied space you can see.
	
**Spells (Light Beams).** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: faerie fire (1 charge), daylight (3 charges), sickening radiance (4 charges), wall of light (5 charges), holy weapon (5 charges), dawn (5 charges), sunbeam (6 charges), crown of stars (7 charges), holy aura (8 charges), or sunburst (8 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Light Speed).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Time Stop, without expending any charges or material components. You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.



```
```




##### Goro Goro no Mi (Lightning)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Gaseous Logia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A bright blue pineapple with sharp swirling patterns.
	
**Description.** Allows its user to create, control, and transform into lightning at will.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Logia Immunity.** You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through your lightning body. Additionally, you are immune to lightning damage and the deafened condition, as well as resistant to thunder damage.

**Elemental Form.** You can use the "Logia Elemental Form" feature listed under "Designing a Logia Devil Fruit Sheet".
	
**Electric Body.** You learn the Lightning Lure and Shocking Grasp Cantrips, no material components required. Additionally, you can cast witch bolt (1st level) as an action, no charges or material components required. You can cast it at higher levels by spending a devil fruit charge for each additional level the spell is cast at.

**Electromagnetic Surveillance.** You have advantage on Wisdom (Perception) checks that rely on hearing. Additionally, you can expend 1 devil fruit charge cast Clarivoyance with only the ability to hear, no material components required.
	
**Spells (Lightning Strikes).** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: thunderwave (1 charge, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), shatter (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), heat metal (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional charges), thunder step (3 charges), lightning bolt (3 charges), call lightning (3 charges), storm sphere (4 charges), chain lightning (6 charges), control weather (8 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Kingdom Come).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Storm of Vengeance, without expending any charges or material components. You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Hie Hie no Mi (Ice)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Solid Logia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A long white and blue sharp fruit shaped like an icicle with sharp swirling patterns.
	
**Description.** Allows its user to create, control, and transform into ice at will.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Logia Immunity.** You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through your ice body. Additionally, you are immune to cold damage and you can move across Difficult Terrain created by ice or snow without spending extra Movement.

**Elemental Form.** You can use the "Logia Elemental Form" feature listed under "Designing a Logia Devil Fruit Sheet".
	
**Ice Body.** You learn the Ray of Frost Cantrip, no material components required. Additionally, you can cast ice knife (1st level) as an action, no charges or material components required. You can cast it at higher levels by spending a devil fruit charge for each additional level the spell is cast at.

**Ice Age.** So long as you are conscious, you can walk on water normally as if using the Water Walk spell. Additionally, you can expend 1 devil fruit charge as an action to lower the temperature in a 120-foot-radius sphere centered on a point you can see within 300 feet of you, causing the land, water, and other liquids to freeze over. The ice persists without melting for up to 1 hour or until you destroy it as an action.
	
**Spells (Ice Time).** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: armor of agathys (1 charge, can cast at higher levels by spending additional devil fruit charges), rime's binding ice (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional devil fruit charges), elemental weapon (cold; 3 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional devil fruit charges), ice storm (4 charges), cone of cold (5 charges), otiluke's freezing sphere (6 charges), investiture of ice (6 charges), wall of ice (6 charges), flesh to ice (6 charges; as Flesh to Stone except that the target turns to solid ice with the density and durability of stone), ice capsule (as Power Word: Stun; 8 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Global Ice Age).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Ice Age^ (view Chapter 8 in the Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB), without expending any charges or material components.  You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.



```
```


##### Magu Magu no Mi (Magma)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Liquid Logia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A small bright red and orange melon with a drooping circular swirling pattern.
	
**Description.** Allows its user to create, control, and transform into magma at will.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Logia Immunity.** You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through your magma body. Additionally, you are immune to fire damage and you can move across Difficult Terrain created by rocky terrain or magma without spending extra Movement.

**Elemental Form.** You can use the "Logia Elemental Form" feature listed under "Designing a Logia Devil Fruit Sheet".
	
**Magma Body.** You learn the Lava Splash Cantrip (as Acid Splash, but dealing fire damage instead), no material components required. Additionally, you can cast searing smite (1st level) as an action, no charges or material components required. You can cast it at higher levels by spending a devil fruit charge for each additional level the spell is cast at.
	
**Spells (Red Hound and Eruptions).** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: Hell Armor (as armor of agathys, but dealing fire damage instead; 1 charge, can cast at higher levels by spending additional devil fruit charges), aganazzar's scorcher (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional devil fruit charges), melf's minute meteors (3 charges), erupting earth (3 charges), wall of stone (5 charges), immolation (5 charges), investiture of stone (6 charges), incendiary cloud (8 charges), or meteor swarm (9 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Volcanic Lava.** You can expend 1 devil fruit charge as an action to cause a volcanic eruption in a 30-foot-radius sphere centered on a point you can see within 300 feet of you. After 1d4 rounds at the start of your turn, the surface in that area becomes covered with 1 foot of lava. The lava is considered difficult terrain and deals 10d10 fire damage to any creature that starts its turn in it or enters it for the first time on its turn. The lava also sinks beneath any liquid it enters. This effect lasts for 1 hour, after which the lava hardens into rock.
	
**Awakening (Grand Eruption).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to create a massive volcanic eruption in a 120-foot radius sphere centered on you. Each creature in the radius must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failure, a creature takes 10d10 fire damage, or half as much on a success. Additionally, the ground in the radius is covered in 5-foot deep lava for 1 minute, after which the lava solidifes into 5 feet of solid stone over the ground. Wading through the lava causes a creature to take 10d10 fire damage. Being fully submerged in the lava causes a creature to take 18d10 fire damage. You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.

##### Mera Mera no Mi (Fire)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Gaseous Logia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A bright orange citrus fruit with a swirling flame patterned spikes stemming from its skin.
	
**Description.** Allows its user to create, control, and transform into fire at will.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Logia Immunity.** You are immune to bludgeoning, piercing, and slashing from nonmagical attacks, as physical objects pass through your fire body. Additionally, you are immune to fire damage.

**Elemental Form.** You can use the "Logia Elemental Form" feature listed under "Designing a Logia Devil Fruit Sheet".
	
**Flame Body.** You learn the Fire Bolt, Produce Flame, and Control Flames Cantrips. Additionally, you can cast burning hands (1st level) as an action, no charges or material components required. You can cast it at higher levels by spending a devil fruit charge for each additional level the spell is cast at.

**Burning Wave.** You can expend 1 devil fruit charge as an action to ignite all flammable materials or extinguish all flames within 100 feet of you. Objects or equipment that hold fire, such as torches and lanterns, are suddenly lit. Flammable objects that aren't worn, such those made of wood or wool, catch on fire. A flammable object that is small or smaller is instantly burnt up and reduced to ash. A flammable object that is medium or larger burns at a rate of 1d4 fire damage per round until its fire is put out as an action.
	
**Spells (Flame Commandments).** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: hellish rebuke (1 charge, can cast at higher levels by spending additional devil fruit charges), flaming sphere (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional devil fruit charges), heat metal (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional devil fruit charges), scorching ray (2 charges, can cast at higher levels by spending additional devil fruit charges), fireball (3 charges), ashardalon’s stride (3 charges), wall of fire (4 charges), fire shield (warm shield; 4 charges), flame strike (5 charges), investiture of flame (6 charges), fire storm (7 charges), or incendiary cloud (8 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Flame Emperor).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Flame Emperor^ (view Chapter 8 in the Dungeons and Devil Fruits PHB), without expending any charges or material components. You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.




  



CHAPTER 7 | DEVIL FRUITS & HAKI

\page



##### Yami Yami no Mi (Darkness)
*Devil Fruit, Legendary*

**Type.** Special Logia
	
**Fruit appearance.** A light-purple fruit with upward swirling teardrop protrusions stemming from its skin.
	
**Description.** Allows its user to create, control, and transform into darkness at will.
	
**Sea Weakness.** You are weak to water and seastone.

**Darkness Immunity.** You are immune to necrotic damage, but vulnerable to every other damage type. You also gain darkvision up to 120 feet, and can see through magical darkness.

**Black Spiral.** As an action, you can target a creature within 60 feet of you, attempting to pull it closer to you using intense gravity from your darkness. The target must succeed on a Strength saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or be pulled up to 60 feet toward you and become grappled by you. While it is grappled this way, it is restrained by the darkness in your palm until the grapple is broken.

**Black Hole.** As an action, you may spend 1 or more devil fruit charges to form a large pool of darkness on the ground around you. If you do so, you target each creature and object in a 10-foot-radius sphere centered on you must succeed on a Costitution saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC. A creature takes 3d10 necrotic damage on a failed save and becomes banished into your darkness (as if using the banishment spell, no concentration required) for 1 minute, or half as much damage and doesn't get banished on a successful one. An unworn or unheld object in the radius is automatically banished into the darkness. A creature banished into your darkness is freed if you are reduced to 0 hit points or fall unconscious, reappearing in its original space after it is freed. A creature banished this way has all of it's devil fruit abilities and active effects nullified for the duration. The darkness's damage increases by 1d10 and it's radius increases by 5 feet for each additional devil fruit charge expended over 1, dealing up to 11d10 necrotic damage and having up to a 50-foot radius in total.

**Liberation.** As an action, you can free any object or creature banished into your darkness. If a creature or object is freed this way, it is thrown up to 60 feet in a random direction and knocked prone. If a thrown target strikes a solid surface, the target takes 3 (1d6) bludgeoning damage for every 10 feet it was thrown. If the target is thrown at another creature, that creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw against your Devil Fruit save DC or take the same damage and be knocked prone.

**Darkness Storage.** Your carrying capacity is multiplied by 100, as you are able to store objects within black holes on your body. Any object you carry that isn't being worn or held is stored in a pocket dimension (as if using a bag of holding) which can only be released by you. If you fall unconscious or drop to 0 hit points, all objects you are storing in your pocket dimension is released from your body.

**Devil Fruit Nullification.** When a creature is restrained or grappled by you or a spell cast by this devil fruit, it is unable to use any devil fruit abilities for the duration of the grapple or restraint, and any active devil fruit effects it was using are suddenly ended, as if the creature was touched by seastone. 
	
**Spells (Black Hole).** This devil fruit power has 17 charges. You can expend 1 or more of its charges to cast one of the following spells from it without needing to expend material components: absorb elements (1 charge), darkness (2 charges), vortex warp (2 charges), hunger of hadar (3 charges), pulse wave (3 charges), shadow of moil (4 charges), evard's black tentacles (4 charges), banishment (4 charges), destructive wave (necrotic; 5 charges), circle of death (6 charges), dark star (8 charges). The devil fruit regains expended charges daily at dawn.
	
**Awakening (Infinity Black Hole).** Once you've awakened your power, you can use an action to cast Ravenous Void, without expending any charges or material components. You can’t use this action again for another 24 hours.




CHAPTER 4 | LEGENDARY LOGIA
